Northeast Prepares to Commemorate the Martyrs

Shenyang Correspondence: In the recent Sino-Russian war, our side suffered a great number of casualties. In order to commemorate the loyal and righteous and to comfort the heroic souls, the provincial and municipal legal entities are preparing a large-scale memorial service. A preparatory meeting was held at the General Chamber of Commerce at 6:00 PM on the 25th. Representatives from the General Chamber of Commerce, the Foreign Affairs Association, the Youth Association, the Education Association, the Agricultural Association, the National Common Sense Promotion Association, the Lawyers Association, the Morality Association, and various schools and newspapers, totaling over 40 people, attended. Jin Zhezhen, the president of the General Chamber of Commerce, reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that this memorial service was to commemorate the soldiers who died in the defense against Russia. The Sino-Russian war was an international war, and the soldiers who sacrificed their lives for the country were of great value and unprecedented in the past 30 years. The fallen leaders included Brigade Commander Han Guangdi, Deputy Brigade Commander Wei of Liang Zhongjia's brigade, and the two regimental commanders, Lin and Zhang. There were also thousands of lower-ranking officers and soldiers. The association began organizing in December of the 18th year. When the Northeastern authorities held a military conference earlier, this matter was discussed. Chairman Wan of Heilongjiang Province scheduled a memorial service for April 5th at the Martyrs' Shrine in Longsha Park, Jiang Province, and has telegraphed the entire country to solicit eulogies and has established a preparatory committee, appointing Du Hongnian, the counselor of the National Defense Preparatory Office, as the director of the preparatory office, Section Chief Li of the Staff Office as the accountant, Section Chief E of the National Defense Office as the person in charge of soliciting contributions, and Section Chief Zhang of the Adjutant Office as the person in charge of general affairs. The duties of literary style are jointly undertaken by Secretary He and Section Chief Meng of the National Defense Office. In addition, there are several adjutants and staff members assisting in the handling. The province is now also planning to hold the memorial service simultaneously on April 5th. When Superintendent Mo Liuzhen went south recently, he mentioned this matter to various dignitaries of the National Government. The National Government then realized the truth and planned to honor the fallen Brigade Commander Han and cast a bronze statue of Han in the Central Park in Nanjing. Commander Zhang has now collected Han's articles and works and sent them to the Northeast University Factory to print 10,000 copies to be distributed to various legal entities and organizations as a permanent commemoration. The address of the memorial service is planned to be held at Xiaoheyan. After the establishment of this preparatory committee, it will telegraph the National Government and the party headquarters of various provinces and cities to solicit elegiac couplets. The content of the preparatory committee has been decided by public discussion to be divided into eight departments: publicity, general affairs, lectures, discipline, investigation, supervision, reception, and ceremonies. Nineteen committee members were elected: Jin Zhezhen, Lu Naigeng, Yan Yuheng, Bian Zongmeng, Wang Jingxuan, Guo Daofu, Zhang Youqi, Wang Zhuchen, Yu Zhishu, Guan Sijiu, Li Hanwu, Mei Foguang, Song Xugang, Wang Zihua, Li Mengxing, Wang Xiushan, Chen Xianyi, Yan Weitang, and Ji Jinsheng. After the election, it was decided that the entire city would lower flags to half-mast on the day of the memorial service, observe five minutes of silence, and cease all work activities, and send letters to various counties to hold the memorial service simultaneously. (26th)

Continued Exchange Measures for Shanxi Currency Not Announced

Those Exchanging Cash Are Still Very Crowded

Taiyuan Correspondence: Since the Shanxi currency was suspended again, the exchange rate has continued to rise, increasing from 8 yuan to 22 yuan in just a few days. If it continues to rise, it will return to the original state of 26 yuan last year. As for soaring prices, one can imagine. The people have been in a state of panic in recent days, and public discussions have regarded the exchange as a major social issue. The authorities have held many meetings recently and had previously planned to allow arbitrary exchange for those under 50 yuan and to require a 40% deduction for financial bonds for those over 50 yuan. This plan is still under review and has not been announced to the public. Yesterday, Meng Yuanwen of the Financial Public Bond Committee, under the order of the Provincial Government, convened Qiu Yangjun, the Director of Civil Affairs, Li Shangren, the Director of Industry and Commerce, Yuan Hongji, the Director of Public Security, Wang Zhaotai, the President of the General Chamber of Commerce, and others to hold a meeting to discuss and decide on eight measures to crack down on unscrupulous merchants who undermine the exchange of provincial currency, which are recorded as follows: (1) The number of banknotes issued by the Provincial Bank must be accurately determined and the issuance of additional banknotes shall be temporarily suspended thereafter; (2) The banknotes exchanged shall be reported to the Provincial Government on a daily basis and temporarily sealed by the Provincial Bank; (3) A separate address shall be found for the exchange and registration shall be made one day in advance, and the exchange shall be carried out in order the following day; (4) The daily exchange shall be limited to 400 numbers; (5) Each number shall not exchange more than 200 yuan; (6) Exchange shall be carried out by matching the issuance of financial public bonds; (7) Discounting of banknotes is prohibited; (8) Raising the exchange rate is strictly prohibited. It is also reported that the authorities have stated that during the previous period of exchange of provincial currency, it was crowded every day, and the staff of the Provincial Bank were unable to handle it. Moreover, those holding currency for exchange have inevitably been turned away in recent days, and these people holding currency for exchange are not only merchants and residents of the provincial capital, but also a majority of those coming to the province from various counties holding currency. In order to unify the measures, once all the procedures for the continued exchange of this provincial currency are in place, it is planned to order the branches and outposts of the Provincial Bank in the outer counties to handle it in the same way as in the province. This is currently being planned. (February 28th)

Provisional Measures for Anhui Northern Militia

Bengbu Dispatch: Northern Anhui has long been a bandit-infested area. The people of each county, in order to defend themselves, have formed People's Self-Defense Corps. The Anhui Provincial Government's temporary office in Bengbu, in order to reorganize them, has specially drafted eleven provisional measures for handling the militia in the 21 counties of northern Anhui. They were specially brought up for discussion at the Northern Anhui Rehabilitation Conference and have already been passed. The articles are as follows: (1) These measures are based on the National Government's promulgated National Defense Law and the Provincial Government's resolution, which was submitted to the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Military Affairs and Ministry of Interior for record. They are the Reorganization Plan for People's Self-Defense Corps, and are formulated with reference to local conditions. (2) Each county magistrate is instructed to report to the office and the prefectural office within seven days of receiving this document, detailing whether there have been any changes in the militia in the county during this incident, the course of events, the losses, and the number of firearms still in existence, for verification and decision. (3) Each county magistrate is instructed to reorganize the militia under their jurisdiction as soon as possible after receiving this document in order to maintain治安. (4) In accordance with the National Government's clear order and with reference to the Henan precedent, all militia below the county level shall be renamed "Defense Corps." No other names shall be used to prevent confusion. (5) The Defense Corps shall be organized into Regular and Reserve units. If the existing 7,965 rifles, Mauser pistols, light mortars, and machine guns, etc. of the Regular units of each county are insufficient, they may be borrowed from the people. (6) Each county magistrate is instructed to ascertain the number of existing sophisticated weapons in the county, and, in accordance with the army organization and local conditions, organize a number of Regular Corps teams under the command and dispatch of the county magistrate. They must effectively cooperate with neighboring counties in joint defense and mutual assistance. The joint defense regulations shall be formulated by the county magistrates. (7) Each county magistrate shall, in the shortest possible time, supervise the district chiefs,保甲, etc. to be responsible for organizing the Reserve Corps in accordance with the Defense Corps Law to supplement the inadequacy of the Regular Corps. (8) The expenses of the Self-Defense Corps in each county shall be uniformly managed by the county magistrate through the local financial management office. If there are any cases of embezzlement or misappropriation, the county magistrate shall deal with them in accordance with the law at any time. (9) The Provincial Government's temporary office in Bengbu shall, based on the resolutions of the Rehabilitation Conference, request the Provincial Government to abolish the district corps chief system. (10) If a local team is accused of being involved in the rebellion, the county magistrate shall secretly investigate whether they were willing participants or were coerced, and whether there is concrete evidence of disrupting order. Proposals shall be made separately and reported for approval. Accusations made by individuals shall not be considered in order to appease those who are wavering and reduce disputes. (11) If there are any matters not covered in these measures, the Regular Corps shall be handled with reference to the Reorganization Plan for People's Self-Defense Corps, and the Reserve Corps shall be handled in accordance with the Defense Corps Law. If there are any doubts, they shall be submitted to the Provincial Government for instructions.

The Process of Monitoring Lu Dangping

Tianjin Dispatch: Lu Dangping, member of the Tianjin Municipal Party Reorganization Committee and concurrently Minister of Propaganda, has been working diligently since taking office. He has issued various slogans with sharp language. Lu is also dissatisfied with the actions of the Shanxi faction and often expresses his views. On February 24, the military and political authorities suddenly received a telegram from Yan Xishan, instructing them to pay attention to the Party headquarters' activities. On the afternoon of February 26, at 6 p.m., Lu was suddenly placed under surveillance by armed police from the Second Special District. At the time, it was only said that there were rumors of actions detrimental to Lu, so police were dispatched for protection. Lu's freedom of movement was restricted, and he could not meet with guests. Other members of the Reorganization Committee, Liu Butong and Chen Shiquan, were shocked upon hearing the news and immediately fled to the French Concession that night. After Lu was placed under surveillance, he immediately sent a letter to Mayor Cui Tingxian requesting assistance. Cui replied the next morning, saying that Commander Fu had always treated people with sincerity and kindness, and that he was compelled to act by orders and asked Lu to relax and assured him that there was no danger. After receiving the letter, Lu sent another letter to Cui asking him to find a way to restore his freedom and await a thorough investigation. That afternoon, he was able to meet with guests. Since then, the staff of the Municipal Party Headquarters have fled, leaving only one or two irresponsible employees in the Propaganda Department, Organization Department, Training Department, Civil Training Committee, and Secretariat to guard the documents. Public Security Bureau Chief Zeng Yanxi went to the Municipal Party Headquarters at 4 p.m. to talk to the staff who remained, saying that the detention of Minister Lu was a personal matter, not a Party matter, nor a Social Affairs Bureau matter. He asked everyone to work with peace of mind and continue to be responsible. Although someone has come to negotiate the takeover of the Municipal Party Headquarters, it cannot be handed over without a solid basis or an order from Commander-in-Chief Yan. He ordered the five districts and three precincts to tighten the restrictions on the Municipal Party Headquarters, forbidding all guests from entering. Even internal personnel were required to have badges to enter and exit. In the evening, the Eighth District Party Headquarters distributed leaflets criticizing Chen Shiquan, Minister of Organization, for manipulating the election. At the time, rumors circulated that Chen had been arrested at the station, but investigations later proved this to be false.

Mayor Cui Tingxian issued a handwritten order on the evening of the 27th, appointing Feng Sizhi, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, as acting Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, and promoted Liu Jinxuan, a technician, to Assistant in the Secretariat. Feng went to the Social Affairs Bureau on the afternoon of the 28th to assume his duties and summoned the staff of each section to give a speech, saying that he was acting in this position and hoped that everyone would continue to serve with peace of mind.

After Lu Dangping was placed under surveillance, the Garrison Command, in order to dispel external misunderstandings, released the telegram from Taiyuan regarding the handling of Lu's case at midnight. It is recorded as follows: "To Commander Fu of Tianjin, Highly Confidential: We have intercepted a telegram from Lu Dangping of Tianjin to Chen Lifu in Nanjing, stating, 'Please present to the Chairman for his consideration, today Shi secretly copied the full text of the telegram from Li, Huang, Zhang, and Bai to Yan, telegram to Commander-in-Chief Yan Xishan of Taiyuan for his consideration, having read the telegram urging Chiang to step down to apologize to the people of the country, I am pleased to share the same sentiments, I am deeply grateful, but Chiang is selfish and self-serving, and obstinately refuses to repent, I hope to use force to pursue his withdrawal, the initial intention of peace can be ensured, the Southern Righteous Army should follow in your footsteps, I dare to declare my innermost feelings, I cannot express my remote aspirations, Li Zongren, Huang Shaoxiong, Bai Chongxi, Zhang Fakui, etc. kowtow to request deletion.' After investigating, Yan is insidious and has repeatedly caused chaos, all with their background, if it is not clearly ordered to be denounced, the disaster is endless, if the Central Government transports troops by sea and blocks Tianjin and Tanggu, then they have no way, speed is of the essence, delay will be difficult to plan, also, Pingdeng's work, I feel very difficult in the environment, the staff of the telegraph bureau have secretly subsidized 100 yuan, Shi is the one who investigates the other party's news, monthly salary of 80 yuan, the party's activity funds are too small, can the Chair send a certain amount of temporary fees to facilitate inquiring about all the news, in case of emergency, prepare to move to the concession to work, and please the Central Government to send people to install a radio station in Tianjin to avoid the telegram being seized, etc. Especially reach, hope to investigate for important matters, Yan Xing reply."

Liu Lianyi, Member of the Shandong Provincial Reorganization Committee, Assassinated

At 5:00 p.m. on the 4th, Liu Lianyi, a member of the Shandong Provincial Reorganization Committee and concurrently Minister of Organization, was assassinated inside the Preparatory Office of the National Qingdao University in Baotu Spring. The Shandong Provincial Reorganization Committee had summoned personnel from Party headquarters in various counties to the province for training, totaling more than 100 people, who were working at the Preparatory Office of Qingdao University. On that day, Liu was working in the class and left work at 5:00 p.m. As soon as he exited the small door in the southeast corner of the training class classroom, he saw students playing ball in the courtyard outside the door. Unexpectedly, there were two people outside the door, one acting as a lookout, and the other immediately shot Liu twice, hitting him in the waist. He immediately fell to the ground. At that time, the students in the courtyard shouted in panic, and the assassin calmly escaped. Liu's entourage immediately called various places to report. Min, the director of the public security sub-bureau in charge of the outer city district, was the first to arrive, and important figures from the Provincial Government, the Provincial Reorganization Committee, and the Municipal Party Headquarters all went to visit. On one hand, they ordered the Public Security Bureau and the Garrison Command to quickly arrest the assassin, and on the other hand, they sent Liu to the Jinan Hospital for treatment by car. At 7:00, Zhai Yuqing, a student from the training class, was arrested, and a pistol was found in his possession, making him a prime suspect. He was sent to the General Headquarters for strict interrogation. Zhai is from Yanggu County. After Liu arrived at Jinan Hospital, surgery was performed in the surgical department. According to Liu Zhongming, secretary of the Organization Department, Minister Liu was shot twice in the waist, from back to front. The bullets were Browning type, while Zhai Yuqing's gun was not a Browning. It was also said that Liu's injuries were quite serious and the danger period had not yet passed. The bullets passed through his waist from behind and fell into his clothes.

Fuzhou Money Shop Redemption Problem

Money Shop Public Association Agrees on Relief Measures

Market Overcomes Important Period Steadily

Fuzhou Dispatch: The banknotes issued by the Fuzhou money shops previously, because the Provincial Government ordered them to be directly redeemed, lacked prepared cash, fearing a run on the banks. It was proposed to gradually reduce the amount of大洋 in circulation and issue a kind of "virtual standard" banknotes or commercial bank notes for use in transferring funds between shops. Society opposed this, seeing it as disrupting the currency system and harming finance. Now, this "virtual standard" silver note has been banned by order of the Provincial Government's Currency Law Committee, and the money shops are instructed to: (1) All banknotes issued in the future should still be based on the大洋. (2) This大洋 note should be directly redeemed. (3) For the exchange of banknotes for silver dollars, no premium or surcharge may be requested. The money shops, seeing the agitation of society and the severity of the official attitude, had no choice but to comply and abolish the proposal for silver notes, continuing to issue small silver notes. Starting from March 1, direct redemption was implemented. The price of大洋 was forty or fifty文 higher per dollar than the banknotes, so a premium was required for exchanging notes for silver dollars. This is now gradually falling, becoming the same price as banknotes. However, the ready cash of each money shop is insufficient to supply the large amount of banknotes needed by the market. If all大洋 notes are issued, the problem of simultaneous redemption would be difficult to resolve. Therefore, the Money Shop Public Association has agreed on two relief measures: (1) Only five kinds of大洋 notes will be issued: one dollar, two dollars, three dollars, five dollars, and ten dollars for circulation in the market. (2) For shops who draw notes from the money shops for use in transferring funds, another kind of大洋 white slip starting from a minimum of one hundred dollars in whole numbers will be issued, which will still be redeemed归枰 (meaning the note holder cannot directly redeem from the issuing bank, but shops owing money to the money shop can use this slip to pay off the debt, and each money shop can redeem it themselves.) (3) The government is requested to use silver dollars for the collection of donations and taxes and the issuance of new salaries. The operations of the two national banks, the Central Bank and the Bank of China, and the two foreign banks, HSBC and the Bank of Taiwan, should all use silver dollars. All money shops should use silver dollars for buying and selling Hong Kong and Shanghai drafts. All should not accept大洋 notes, so as to reduce circulation. The Currency Law Committee is currently considering these two proposals. In addition, there is one other matter that is closely related to finance, namely, the price of small silver coins in the city. Each coin was previously worth more than 80文. Since the Provincial Government started minting 20-cent subsidiary coins at the Majiang Silver Dollar Bureau, the price of small silver coins has fallen accordingly, and each coin is now worth only 75文 and cannot be maintained. The livelihood of the common people has been greatly affected, reportedly due to the low quality of the coins. Yesterday, the Currency Law Committee decided to submit a request to the Provincial Government to make the auxiliary coins publicly assayed to show good faith.

As for the market situation in the city, due to the redemption crisis at the end of the lunar year, credit was tight, and turnover was slow. Various merchants went bankrupt one after another, totaling about two million dollars, of which the money merchants suffered the greatest losses from their loans. The second day of the second lunar month, the beginning of the business year, was an important transition period for the market. Merchants, seeing the market depression, anticipated that the shops might have a severe shake-up during that period, and in advance, they specially instructed various brokers to go to each shop to earnestly negotiate that, no matter what, the most important thing was to try their best to maintain the status quo and not to lightly abandon the situation and resort to the inferior tactic of closing shop and fleeing. If they were short of funds by the due date, the merchants were willing to reduce the amount of interest due and wait until after this second day of the lunar month to gradually make up for it, so as not to lose all their capital. The shop would also not collapse. In addition, after that period, the money merchants' old debts could be settled, and new discounts could be issued again. The matter hung by a thread, all depending on this. The shopkeepers also felt that since the merchants were willing to be accommodating, the opportunity for recovery could be avoided. Therefore, the market conditions in the city were able to overcome the difficult period steadily. (March 3)

Resolutions of the Third Plenary Session

Suggestion from the Jiangsu Provincial Party Reorganization Committee to the Central Government to Establish a Foundation for National Direct Trade with National Power

Upon investigation, our country's foreign trade is almost entirely controlled by foreigners. Therefore, our country's goods often cannot freely compete with foreign goods in the world market. Within the country, the procurement and collection of goods are mostly done by foreigners employing our compatriots to do the work for them, and the manipulation and monopoly in between often cause producers or small merchants to suffer. When goods leave the country, they pass through the hands of many parties, and all the profits go to foreigners. Even the name of the place of origin does not belong to our country, which is truly distressing. This is caused by the failure of national policy and the morality of former merchants, as well as various reasons for economic inadequacy. This situation is a great loss to the country's economy and a major obstacle to promoting national products. If we cannot obtain an international commercial position, the so-called promotion of national products will be limited to within the country. Foreign industrial and commercial circles can still plan their opportunities for aggression and oppression at any time. How can this passive approach be sustainable? It is necessary for our country's goods to first obtain an international position, and then proceed to promote them to the outside world, so that the use of patching up leaks will be greatly effective. As for the great plan of establishing a nation, it is even more indispensable. Examining Japan, its situation in the past was the same as our country's today. The adoption of direct trade methods was not long ago, but today it is active all over the world. The adoption of this method is closely related to the adequacy of the economy, so it cannot be established without national power.

Suggestion from the Jiangsu Provincial Party Reorganization Committee to Thoroughly Reorganize the National Tax System and Collection Methods within a Time Limit, Eliminate All Malpractices, and Use National or Local Banks as Tax Collection Agencies to Establish the Independence of the Treasury

Upon investigation, our country's finances, since the Republic of China, have been chaotic layer by layer, almost beyond repair. Fortunately, our Party has overcome everything with its ideology, put down rebellions, and settled military affairs, which is a good opportunity to reorganize finances. In the past, the investigation of the chaos of finances, its main cause is still in the system and the order. If the system is not good, loopholes are everywhere and become the origin of many malpractices in a bad social environment. If the order is not strict, then everything is chaotic, and there is no way to check. Those who cheat can do things calmly. Taking land tax as an example, the鱼鳞 archives are often incomplete, or based on strings of numbers, or relying on cabinet books, and the debts of the people and the losses of the officials cannot be investigated. As for tax collection, it is either contracted or collected, without a fixed method. Ticket books and inspections are even more muddled, so that outsiders cannot understand clearly, nor can they get an inkling of what is underneath. What is even more harmful to merchants and the people is the likin customs checkpoints, where malpractices abound, and they can do their utmost to extort and demand. If there is a good system, and strict audit and investigation are carried out, and if we can do our best to turn private into public, then the income of the nation and local areas will surely increase greatly. This can be said with certainty. Also, examining the biggest malpractice in finance, the collection, expenditure, and safekeeping are all managed by one agency, and the intermingling and misappropriation therein can further encourage corruption. Therefore, we specially suggest formulating a system, eliminating malpractices, and stipulating that national or local banks should be used as tax collection agencies to establish the independence of the treasury. This is the key strategy for reorganizing finances.

Suggestion by Committee Members Kong Xiangxi, Sun Ke, and Liu Jiwen to Define Increasing Work Efficiency, Developing Industrial Production, Enlightening Workers' Knowledge, Maintaining Workers' Health, and Connecting Workers' Friendship as the Work Standards for Labor Organizations during the Period of Political Tutelage

Regarding the proposal: I believe that at the beginning of political tutelage, construction is in full swing. All of our countrymen should strive to build a foundation for the country. Laborers should also shoulder the responsibility of major construction work. What is the work? Strive to create production to enrich the country's economy. This construction work should be actively sought by labor organizations to benefit themselves and others, but also depends on the consistent supervision and guidance of the central Party and government agencies. Therefore, when the National Government settled the whole country, it strived to reorganize labor organizations to improve their organization and should especially provide guidance according to the times, so that they can engage in construction and devote themselves to the development of production to build a solid foundation for the national economy. Examining various European and American countries, due to the abnormal development of capitalism, laborers are exploited by it, and the government lacks good ways to eliminate and remedy the situation, resulting in laborers having a reaction to seek their own interests through organizations. However, our Party builds the country with the Three Principles of the People and implements a policy for all people. All people from all walks of life with occupations should be protected and cared for without discrimination, so that all people have a spirit of cooperation, and labor and capital have no hidden worries of division. Moreover, our country's production is backward, industry and commerce are declining, and there are frequent disasters, and all industries have been abandoned. We should unite the spirit of the entire nation, help each other, cooperate, and strive together to fight to the death against foreign enemies with aggressive economic policies, and should not divide ourselves into classes, disperse our forces, and create unnecessary disturbances to cut off our own chances of survival. Previously, during the military government period, domestic obstacles had not been removed. Generally, comrades in the labor world, driven by patriotic enthusiasm, in order to gather revolutionary forces, initiated demonstrations of strikes and slowdowns, giving a serious blow to the warlord government, with the aim of promoting national unity and helping the success of the revolution. Their intentions were very good, and the results were significant. Now, times have changed, and the situation is very different. Those who held negative ideas in the past should now change and hold a positive attitude, and those who used destructive methods in the past should now change and engage in construction work. The so-called construction work, in detail, is how to increase work efficiency, how to develop industrial production, how to enlighten workers' knowledge, how to maintain workers' health, and how to connect workers' friendship. All of these are important issues for the workers themselves. They should use a peaceful, quiet, persevering, and resilient spirit, holding the purpose of self-governance, self-improvement, achieving themselves, and achieving others, and seek continuous progress in workers and industry. They should also unite with industrial and commercial enterprises across the country to jointly plan progress and compete in the world market. If they do not know what they are doing, mistakenly take the standard, and want to divide the remaining benefits from the so-called capitalists in the country who are dying to improve their lives and raise their positions, not only is it like climbing a tree to catch fish and will never be possible, but it will also see that domestic production is even more backward, and the wealth of the entire nation will be even more depleted. The direction is completely different from the desired goal. In the past, Germany implemented an eight-hour workday before the European War. After the defeat in the war, the national economy was on the verge of collapse. Workers were concerned about the difficulties of the time and tried to save the situation. The working hours were automatically increased to twelve hours. The rise and fall of the country is the responsibility of every citizen. Efforts to produce, to strengthen the foundation of the country, the German people's good deeds, is the model of our country, to draw from the party's ideology, is to work for the freedom and equality, mutual aid throughout China, so as to achieve the purpose, so that those who live in it, lives can be improved, the position can be enhanced, otherwise foreign aggression occurs frequently, internal trouble will rise again, and want to seek the benefits of a class at this time, the so-called皮之不存、毛将焉附, not only violates the party's ideology, but also has no way to complete alone. Xiangxi believes that the standard of labor movement in the future is extremely important, it must be "striving to build the cause, as the work standard of labor organizations" can avoid going astray, can notify political party agencies, based on this standard, actively promote and guide, strive to carry out, so that the future of political tutelage, production cause, smooth operation, the happiness of all the people, the blessing of the party and the country, is there any due, respectfully waiting for public resolution,

Kong Xiangxi, Sun Ke, Liu Jiwen Three Committee Members Submit the Proposal to Raise Capital Construction Funds

The establishment of the capital and the initiation of construction, setting a model for the whole country and enhancing the views of friendly countries, are of great importance and need not be said. However, the initial operation depends on funding. The capital is jointly owned by the people of the whole country, and its funding should be borne by the people of the whole country. The capital construction committee has now drafted an outline for the construction plan. Once the funds are raised, they can be implemented. Funds should be raised immediately to start construction. It is estimated that the minimum construction funding should be 50 million yuan, based on the national average burden, taking into account the economic situation of various provinces and regions, separately raising 30 million yuan in public debt and allocating 20 million yuan from various provinces and regions, and raising the full amount in the shortest possible time so that capital construction can be completed as soon as possible. A proposal for raising and allocating funds is hereby prepared as follows. Is there anything appropriate, respectfully waiting for public resolution. (Methods) (1) Issuance of Public Debt: The Ministry of Finance will issue 30 million yuan in capital construction public debt, issued in two phases. The first phase is 10 million yuan, and the second phase is 20 million yuan. The principal and interest fund are guaranteed by the customs surplus. (2) Allocation to Various Provinces and Regions: Based on the amount of land tax in each province and the size of the region, they are divided into five grades for allocation, bearing a total of 20 million yuan, to be paid off in three years. The amount allocated to each province and region is listed separately below.

Implementation of County Organization Law in Zhejiang Province

Strict Deadline for Completion by the End of June This Year

The Zhejiang Provincial Government, after careful consideration of the implementation of the county organization law, considering that the local conditions of the counties in the province are different, should review the case of the Zhejiang County Organization Law Modification Handling with the affiliated bureaus and offices, and then the Provincial Government will review and resolve the issue in a meeting. The first phase of the reorganization of the county government is allowed to be implemented in stages and will first reorganize and establish the eighteen counties of Hangzhou, Haining, Wuxing, Shaoxing, Jiaxing, Changxing, Xiaoshan, Yuyao, Pinghu, Haiyan, Jiashan, Shangyu, Cixi, Yin County, Zhenhai, Deqing, Chongde, and Tongxiang. The remaining fifty-seven counties will be given additional funding as appropriate. The second phase of delimiting county districts will also be handled separately by the Civil Affairs Department in accordance with the implementation deadline decided by the National Government, and the seventy-five county magistrates will be notified to comply, and the department will send personnel to conduct a survey and approve the record. However, the district offices have not been fully organized because the township organizations have not been carried out at the same time, and the third step of preparing for district and township affairs for the implementation of the county organization law will also be delayed. It is now learned that the Provincial Government has received a telegram from the National Government, requiring the province to implement the county organization law and must complete it by the end of June of the 19th year in accordance with the approved extension. It has specially instructed the Civil Affairs Department to inform and strictly urge the county magistrates. It is also heard that a disciplinary measure has been formulated for the county magistrates who are slow to progress in the future to promote supervision.

Wuhu Express News

Due to the current troop deployments, the local political and business circles here consider local security to be extremely important. Yesterday afternoon, a security meeting was specially held at the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The head of the Municipal Administration, the county magistrate, the head of the Public Security Bureau, the head of the Chamber of Commerce, the head of the Self-Defense Corps, and others attended. It was resolved that 90 people would be drawn from the Municipal Public Security Bureau Security Team, 90 people would be drawn from the County Self-Defense Corps, and 72 people would be drawn from the Chamber of Commerce, to be divided into three squadrons, and combined to form the Wuhu Provisional Public Security Brigade. The head of the Public Security Bureau, Yu Mingxun, was appointed as the commander-in-chief, and the head of the Chamber of Commerce, Lu Tingzhen, and the head of the Self-Defense Corps, Ding Shikai, were appointed as deputy commanders. The establishment was announced on the 5th. The command post is located in the old town government office. The officers and soldiers each receive their original salaries. Temporary expenses are to be jointly funded by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the County Government, and the Chamber of Commerce.

The General Headquarters sent a telegram yesterday to inform the local Chamber of Commerce, stating that it had ordered Army Commander Ma of Anqing to send a regiment to Wuhu to take charge of defense duties. A battalion of Ma's troops has now arrived in Pukou to assemble. Ning Xingde.

The Anhui Provincial Preliminary Round of the Central China Games, the ball games of the Second District, have been held at the Public Sports Field for three days since the 2nd, with athletes from various schools braving the rain. The Provincial Department of Education specially sent Supervisor Li Shaoling and Deng Qiang, the Minister of Sports for the entire province, to Wuhu to supervise the competition. It closed yesterday. The overall result is that the Second Vocational High School won the football championship, and the Industrial Vocational School won the basketball championship. The Department of Education has sent telegrams ordering the winning athletes to go to the province to participate before March 11.

The Wuhu County Administrative Conference, which opened on February 20, closed on March 3. Since the appointment of the new Anhui Provincial Government Chairman Ma Fuxiang, some people here have telegraphed to Beijing to welcome him and urged him to come to Anhui as soon as possible to take charge of the government. Recently, a reply telegram from Ma stated that he was still firmly resigning due to illness and could not come to Anhui for the time being.

After the self-defense corps of Dahuajin, Xuezhen and other places in Dangtu were coerced by bandits to seize weapons and escape, County Magistrate Jiang Zhongya led a team to pursue and suppress them. Local Communications

Songjiang

Prohibition of Stealing City Bricks. Several sections of the city wall of this county have collapsed, and pedestrians can freely enter and exit. The official government is unable to repair them, and the collapsed areas are becoming more and more numerous. Recently, some people from Jiangbei have been stealing city bricks and selling them for cash. Over time, many have been stolen. Now, Wang Daochang, Zhang Jingquan and others have submitted a request to the county government for prohibition. The government has already ordered the police to prohibit the theft and issued a notice. If unemployed vagrants are found stealing city bricks, they should be immediately handed over to the police on duty for investigation and prosecution.

Confessions of Liu Xiaomei and Others. The four bandits, Liu Xiaomei, Wang Shaodi, Li Shan, and Jin Ada, were escorted back to the county government of this county by the water police yesterday. After interrogation, the presiding judge Du interrogated the criminals in a preliminary trial. According to the confessions of Liu Xiaomei and others, they are all locals. They confessed to the robbery of Fang Zhengming's cotton boat and the robbery was true. They had pooled 100 yuan with Li Songpo and others, who had already been arrested, and handed it over to a certain person. They also kidnapped meat tickets in Xinzhengbing and Jiaxing. In the Xinzhengbing kidnapping case, they obtained a ransom of 1,500 yuan. After the small steam local security officer Pan Jingqing divided the loot and took 600 yuan, the remainder was divided. The Jiaxing ransom was also divided by the local people, and the remainder was distributed, etc. Jin Ada confessed that he was looking for work in Shanghai. On the night of the arrest, he happened to be playing at Liu's place. He did not know what Liu and others had done at first and had not committed any crimes. He was arrested unjustly, etc. The interrogating official ordered Liu and others to be shackled and imprisoned separately, pending verification and handling.

Suzhou

Attempted Suicide Foiled and Rescued. A young man named Guo Maolin, 19 years old, lived at No. 1 Caijia Garden, Erlang Temple, Nanjing. He was an upper-level clerk in the Secretariat of the Ministry of Military Affairs. On the 28th of last month, he took leave to travel to Hangzhou. One day, he met a woman on the train from Hangzhou to Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai, they stayed in a hotel together. Unexpectedly, the woman took Guo's luggage, a camera, and more than 60 yuan in cash, and left. Guo, feeling ashamed to face anyone, attempted suicide by jumping into the river at the Bund in the French Concession. He was rescued and accompanied to the North Station on the 5th, where he was given a ticket and ordered to return to his hometown by train. Who knew that after Guo's train arrived at Suzhou Station, he got off the train and checked into Room No. 9 of the Suzhou Hotel for the night. The next afternoon, Guo went out alone and wandered around on the road for a long time. When he reached the New Yanmenwai South New Bridge, he saw a toilet and went to the toilet. He used hemp rope to hang himself from the beam. He was rescued and lowered by someone. He had not died. After passers-by inquired about his background, he claimed to be staying at the Suzhou Hotel. So he was escorted to the hotel. Xue Yunlong, the manager of the hotel, saw that Guo's clothes were wet from the rain and noticed that his attitude had changed. He inquired with the person who came with him and learned that he had attempted suicide. Fearing that Guo would still have an accident, he reported it to the Fifth Precinct. Patrol Officer Gu Haoru took the police to the scene and took Guo, a bamboo basket, and a hemp rope to the police station. Zhang, the clerk, interrogated him. Because Guo's situation was pitiful, he sent a police officer to accompany him to the station that night and handed him over to the soldier on the train to take Guo back to Nanjing.

The Case of the Patrol Officer Causing Death is Remanded for Retrial. In the town of Wu Guijing, a gentry family surnamed Wang had items stolen by a petty thief named Sun some years ago. He was arrested by Gu Shurong, the patrol officer in charge of the public security sub-station, who released him after private interrogation and beating, resulting in his death. The local court sent personnel to inspect the body. After further inspection by Li Baokun, it was confirmed that Sun died as a result of his injuries. The court then detained Patrol Officer Gu and opened a trial. As a result, he was sentenced to seven years and six months of imprisonment. Gu refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court. The final trial upheld the original verdict. Gu refused to accept the verdict and hired lawyer Yao Yuangui to appeal to the Supreme Court, which immediately approved the appeal and remanded the case for retrial. The High Court held a hearing yesterday (7th) afternoon, presided over by Huang Bingdao, the presiding judge of the Third Tribunal. The original inspector Li Baokun was summoned to the court to state the process. Lawyer Yao defended him and set a date for sentencing.

Wuxi Water Police Escort and Take Custody of Huang Laojunzi. The 14th Team of the 3rd District of the Water Public Security Bureau apprehended a lake bandit named Huang Dechang (aka Huang Laojunzi) who was involved in robbery in Xueyanqiao in Wujiang County on the 3rd of this month. After District Chief Gong interrogated him, Huang confessed to robbery and kidnapping. District Chief Gong immediately sent a letter to the Second District of Wuxi. After receiving the letter, District Chief Mao ordered Captain Zhu Yulin to come to Suzhou yesterday (7th) to escort and take custody of Huang Dechang for investigation and handling.

Fengxian

Police Team Captures Thieves in the Rain. Yang Xingsheng, the captain of the Third Squad of the County Police, captured the long-time bandit Dai and his son-in-law at Daijiaqiao. According to their confessions, there are still many accomplices. He went to continue the search early yesterday morning and discovered a bandit den near the area. In addition to capturing a bandit named Chen Baitou on the spot, he also seized items robbed from various places, as well as various types of spent bullet casings. Captain Yang led the team to investigate. According to the confessions, there are eight accomplices in Shanghai who have scheduled a robbery. All the firearms were secretly transported by them, etc. Yang immediately led the police in the rain to continue the search in various places and did not return until 12 o'clock today.

Collecting Household Population Donations. Because of the unrest in the county, the police force was weak and insufficient for defense. It was decided by County Magistrate Hong Ruisheng to organize a temporary police company for protection. The provincial government has approved the establishment of the company. The first step is to collect the decided household population donation to fund the company. The rate is set at one dime per household for the first month and half of that for the second, third, and fourth months. Yesterday, the district offices were ordered to collect the donations according to the household population register within a time limit.

Qingpu

Ding Songxing's Daughter's Wedding is Robbed and Kidnapped. The family of Ding Songxing, a farmer in Zhushe Village, Fifth District of Qingpu, held a wedding for his daughter the day before yesterday. Guests filled the house, and a grand feast was held. Unexpectedly, while the guests were raising their glasses and drinking happily, more than 20 bandits suddenly arrived, ransacked the boxes and cabinets, and stopped the guests, robbing them of their clothes and jewelry. Before leaving, they kidnapped Ding's eldest son.

Monster Fetus with Cat's Head and Human Body. The owner of Yongxingxiang Fruit Shop, surnamed Shen, in Matou Street of this county, is from Shaoxing. His wife, surnamed Mou, became pregnant last spring. She gave birth to a creature the night before last. It had a cat's head and a human body, with round black eyes, a pointed small mouth, yellow fur on its face, and a pair of small horns on its forehead. Its fingers were very long, resembling human hands. Neighbors heard the news and gathered to watch. Shen thought it was an ominous sign to give birth to this monster and threw it into the river.

[P Wuxi>

A Series of Robberies. The home of Shen Xiaodi, a resident of Huaixia City, Changda Building, and Xia'an Place in this county, was robbed by bandits the night before last. Unexpectedly, the home of Cheng Yunpo, a resident of Chengxiang Lane, which is known for its reputation, was also suddenly attacked by eight or nine bandits armed with handguns at about 1 o'clock last night. They broke into the house by climbing over the wall and ransacked it thoroughly. They took the loot and fled with a howl after half an hour. Silver coins, clothing, and other items worth about 500 or 600 yuan were robbed.

A Fire in Anzhen Kills One Person. A fire broke out suddenly in Xuxing Grain Store on West Street, Anzhen, Seventh District, at about 4 o'clock yesterday morning. The flames soared into the sky and broke through the roof. The nearby fire brigades rushed to the scene after hearing the news and extinguished the fire after an hour of extinguishing. In this fire, all the houses in the store were reduced to ashes. The total loss is estimated to be more than 2,000 yuan. An apprentice in the store was unable to escape when the fire broke out and died in the fire.

Joint Meeting of Relief Institutions. The directors and preparatory committee members of the county's public relief institutions held a joint meeting at the county government at 5 p.m. yesterday. Five important matters were resolved: (1) It was resolved to elect Hua Wenchuan and Li Guanjie as the president and vice president of the relief institutions. (2) It was resolved to reorganize the Nursery Hall into a nursery, the Puji Hall into a nursing home, the Hengshan Hall into a medical clinic, the Civilian Vocational Training Center into a vocational training center, and the Disabled Center to be temporarily attached to the Vocational Training Center. The orphanage will be postponed until funds are raised before it is officially established. (3) It was resolved that the president of the relief institutions should prepare a budget for the operating expenses of the relief institutions and submit it to the local budget meeting for the 19th year. The expenditure for this year is set at 500 yuan, which will be raised from the local expenses. Citizens are requesting the repair of streets. In the past half-month, Wuxi has experienced consecutive days of thunderstorms and rain, and the weather has not cleared up yet. The streets inside and outside the city have been damaged for many years, and water has accumulated everywhere, causing suffering to pedestrians. The Municipal Preparatory Office specially resolved at the previous office meeting to notify citizens and inform the First District Office to notify the township and town chiefs and deputies to automatically initiate fundraising and provide subsidies, so that the work can be repaired. Citizens Sun Xiying, Wu Tingmei, and others believe that the rickshaw donations collected by the Municipal Office were originally intended for road repairs. Therefore, in the past, the Municipal Office would immediately send workers to repair any damaged streets reported by citizens without requiring citizens to pay any additional fees. Now, the rickshaw donations are as high as more than 1,600 yuan per month, but the streets in the city have not been repaired for a long time. The Municipal Office should quickly repair them and should no longer ask the people to donate money. Yesterday, they sent a letter to the Road Widening Committee requesting Director Sun to handle the matter immediately to alleviate the people's difficulties and improve the city's appearance.

Changzhou

Dispatching Commissioners to Cancel Contract Tax Surcharges. According to the Jiangsu Department of Finance, Li Shaoji, a local resident, filed a complaint alleging that Wu County was collecting various surcharges on the sale of official contracts and inspection contracts, such as 40% for education, 10% for public welfare, and 20% for fire protection, etc. These charges were unreasonable. The Department dispatched inspector Wang Junsun to Changzhou on the 6th to work with the County Government Finance Bureau to issue a notice canceling the surcharges. It also clarified the contract tax rate and various surtaxes that were approved to be collected, clarified the types and amounts, made wooden signs, and hung them up for public knowledge. County Magistrate Zhu believed that the donations for education, public welfare, and fire protection were based on old cases, and that if they were canceled all at once before relief measures were devised, the impact would be significant. In addition to explaining the reasons why they could not be canceled in a telegram to the Civil Affairs, Finance, and Education Departments that night, he also went to the province by car on the morning of the 7th to personally explain everything to the departments and request instructions.

Meeting on Regulating People's Food Supply. The Wu County Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of the rice industry at 2 p.m. on the 6th to discuss ways to regulate the people's food supply due to the rising rice prices. More than a dozen rice industry representatives and chamber of commerce members attended. After discussion, it was concluded that the local autumn harvest last year was poor, and there was not much rice in storage. The price of rice from other places was high, and the supply was scarce. The only way to regulate the supply at present is to purchase small-sized rice in bulk to provide relief so that the market price does not rise again.

Nantong

Strict Urging of Industrial Special Police Brigade to Move to Defense. The Department of Civil Affairs previously ordered the First Brigade of the Nantong-Taizhou-Hai'an Industrial Special Police Brigade to be stationed in Nantong, the Second Brigade to be stationed in Haimen, and the Third Brigade to be stationed in Dongtai. Now, Director Miao believes that the brigade commanders have not complied with the order for two months and has strictly urged them to move to their defense posts as soon as possible.

Police and Militia Jointly Suppress Bandits. Bandits are causing serious disturbances in the Yudong, Sanyi, and Yuxi districts of Nantong, causing great harm. The county government has now dispatched a machine gun team to join the police and militia to encircle and suppress the bandits from the Sibaba in different directions. The bandits retreated after two hours of fierce fighting. County Magistrate Chen believes that the bandits are in contact with pirates from the outer seas and has telegraphed the province to send shallow-water warships to block the pirate ships in ports such as Huanben.

The Finance Bureau Cannot Raise Funds to Pay the Allotments. The Finance Bureau received a telegram from the Department of Finance ordering it to remit 10,000 yuan. The Bureau stated that the national and provincial taxes that should be remitted had already been paid in advance and that there was no way to raise the funds at present. It has telegraphed the Department of Finance in reply.

Ordering Discussion of Group Defense Measures. The Provincial Government believes that bandits and communists are rampant in Tongyi and that it is difficult for the officers and soldiers to defend and suppress them. It has ordered the issuance of group defense measures and ordered immediate discussion, reply, and verification for implementation. County Magistrate Chen has discussed and replied to each district separately for submission and verification.

Jiangyin

Director of Education Dismissed Due to the Education Tide, Offers Three Points in Defense. Lin Youming, Director of the Education Bureau, was dismissed due to the education tide. Lin was unwilling to accept the dismissal and submitted three points to the county government for transfer to the provincial government for defense: (1) Unfair expenditure. The expenses of the county's public schools were borrowed in the name of the school principals, and the surtaxes under the Mangcao item were deducted and repaid. This was done in accordance with the order, and the footing was stable. There was no intention of favoring one over the other. Youming came from a foreign land and was impartial, without villains or relatives. If it is considered that the measures were inappropriate, then there is nothing to be done. (2) Detaining the principals. On December 6, 70 or 80 people came to the bureau, claiming to demand the arrears. They demanded, roared, and threatened until late at night. At that time, they received instructions from the Department of Education to strictly investigate the reactionary circumstances of teachers and staff. Jiangyin was also under special martial law. The principals and others were unreasonably making trouble, which may have had other effects. In short, this case has another hidden effect. There are traces and evidence to be found. (3) Not in accordance with the circumstances. It is not known where the so-called circumstances are. Since the salary demands occurred, one dog barked at a shadow, and a hundred dogs barked at the sound. Flyers and declarations were flying like snowflakes. If Lin Youming's crimes were heinous and irreconcilable, in fact, only three or four people from the Three Division faction initiated it.

The Peach Blossom Township Robbery Case is Solved and Escorted for Interrogation. The home of Qi You, a farmer in Taohuaxiang, Sixth District, was robbed on January 26, with a loss of about 200 or 300 yuan. On the 29th, the victim met the bandit child Zhang Ruilin at the Hefeng Pawnshop in Xushu, Wujin, who was pawning clothes. He was immediately arrested and escorted to the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau for detention. Unexpectedly, he escaped the next day. He was recaptured by the Licheng Security Regiment. Five thieves, Zhang Peisheng, Zhang Peilin, Zhang Chenglin, Xia Gouda, He Jiming, and others, were escorted to the bureau for the case. To search for the original loot and for certain relationships, the suspects and 33 pieces of men's and women's clothing were not escorted to the headquarters until yesterday (5th). According to Zhang Peisheng, Zhang Ruilin is his son. Zhang Peilin ordered him to pawn the items. He did not know about stealing from Qi's home. Peilin initiated the idea. Zhang Chenglin said that he did not know about it beforehand. Xia Gouda and He Jiming both said that they went to Qi's home with Peilin to steal things, and they each used two yuan in silver at the time. After the interrogation, a document will be prepared and transferred to the county for handling.

Zhenjiang

Establishment of Military-Political Security Office. Due to winter defense, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs established a joint military-political office in the provincial capital last year. It has been in operation for several months and has achieved considerable results. Now that the winter defense period has passed, reactionary elements are still inciting chaos. Therefore, the Department of Civil Affairs convened a joint military-political security meeting of the provincial capital at 2 p.m. yesterday, chaired by Zhang Zhongli, the chief of the Third Section of the Department of Civil Affairs. It was proposed that a joint security office must be established to determine the name of the agency. It was decided to name it the Joint Military-Political Security Office of the Jiangsu Provincial Capital. Then, security measures were proposed. It was resolved that the Fifth District of the Water Public Security Brigade would be responsible for reconnaissance and defense in the Jiangbei area, from Shierxu and Guazhou in the north, to Zhongli, Liuxu, Huojiaqiao, Simali, and Gangkou, and to Jiangyin in the south. Several patrol ships were dispatched to patrol back and forth. The Provincial Police Headquarters was responsible for reconnaissance and defense near the provincial capital for dozens of miles inside and outside, from Danyang in the south and its main roads. The Military Police Regiment was responsible for reconnaissance and defense from Gaozhi in the west, to Jurong in the southwest, and its main roads. The County Police Brigade was responsible for reconnaissance and defense from Dantu Town in the east and its main roads. Every day, military and police units were rotated to prepare for emergencies and were dispatched to designated locations for alert. The remaining units were all increased. The Provincial Public Security Bureau was responsible for maintaining order in the provincial capital and for paying close attention and conducting strict patrols. Students from the police school and police instructor school were ordered to assist in everything to ensure the security of the provincial capital.

Requesting the Revocation of the Order to Abolish the Chamber of Commerce Association. The Jiangsu Provincial Five-Committee Committee for Farmers, Industry, Commerce, Women, and Youth believes that the Standing Committee of the Central Committee resolved that the new Chamber of Commerce Law and the Industrial and Commercial Guild Law have been promulgated by the government after being formulated by the Legislative Yuan. From now on, the organization of merchant groups should comply with the newly promulgated laws and regulations. There is no need for the existence of the Merchant and Civilian Association, which was established to meet the needs of the times. After careful discussion, it was felt that there were inconveniences in following the facts of the old Chamber of Commerce and the current situation of merchants and civilians. Therefore, in addition to sending Zhang Daoshen, Chen Ru, and Tang Zhengkao to Beijing to petition for the revocation of the abolition order, they also jointly submitted a memorial to the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee yesterday, stating four reasons why the abolition should not be revoked and requesting that the meeting be reconsidered.

Yangzhou

Xu Zhicang Detained for the Second Time. Xu Zhicang, the husband of Zhu Jingwen, whose suicide case caused a sensation in the city and caused disturbances for half a year, was detained and brought to justice after the county government repeatedly summoned him. After the Yushen Petroleum Company granted him bail pending trial, Xu Zhicang requested the High Court to transfer jurisdiction, but it was not approved. The county government repeatedly summoned him until yesterday (4th) before he appeared in court. After the interrogation, he was suddenly sent to the detention center. He has not been released on bail as of today. Two Cases of Attempted Robbery and Theft. Shuangyuheng Rice Store on Guangchumen Street in this city was tunneled into by thieves the night before last, and they stole three hectoliters of Xian rice. Also, yesterday (4th) at 7 p.m., four people resembling bandits suddenly came to Ren Shou Hospital there. One person knocked on the door and entered, and three people were on guard outside. Unexpectedly, the deputy town chief noticed it and brought the local security officers to arrest them. They chased them to Xiaofu Lane and finally caught one of them. He has now been sent to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau for strict handling according to law.

Detention of Zhenjiang-Tongzhou Postal Zhenban Ferry. Xiaoyou, a Zhenjiang-Tongzhou Company ferry that travels between Zhenjiang and Tongzhou, arrived at the wharf outside Dongguan in Yangzhou from the post office at about 9 o'clock on the 5th. Battalion Commander Li, who purchased a ticket to board the ferry, negotiated with the sailors about the cabin. The tea boy did not understand the local dialect, and there was a misunderstanding between them, resulting in a conflict. The ferry is still being detained, and it is not known how it will be resolved.

Handling Land Registration. The county followed the instructions and orders of the Department of Finance to handle land registration. Yesterday (4th), special instructions were given to the local autonomous district offices. In general, land registration will be handled by the district offices separately, according to district maps. Land that has been inspected and registered is free of charge at the time of registration. Land that has been inspected for six months will be charged as usual. Land that has not been inspected will be charged double.

Pinghu

The Second Company of the Provincial Security Brigade Arrives in Pinghu. After the county government received the Newcang robbery alarm, it sent the Second Platoon of the Security Brigade, which had returned to Pinghu from Newcang the day before, to rescue the area. On the other hand, it telegraphed the province to request the dispatch of large troops to suppress the bandits. After receiving the telegram, the province immediately dispatched the Second Company of the Provincial Security Brigade, led by Battalion Commander Wang. They arrived in Pinghu at about 8 p.m. the day before yesterday and stayed overnight in the Dongmen Cocoon Factory and Yimiao Temple. At 8 a.m. yesterday, Battalion Commander Wang led all the soldiers, accompanied by the county magistrate and the water police, hired a small steamer to go to Newcang to suppress the bandits. The number of troops in this bandit suppression is more than 700. Also, yesterday's report stated that the bandits had extorted 17,000 yuan from Newcang. It is now known that only 7,500 yuan was paid. Two people from Tianjin Silk Shop were injured, but they were not harmed.

Zhapu Railway Station Has Started Construction. The Hangzhou-Zhapu section of the highway is scheduled to be officially opened to traffic on April 1st of the Gregorian calendar, and the stations along the way will be completed within March. It is now known that the construction of Zhapu Railway Station is being prepared and is scheduled to be completed in four weeks.

Hangzhou

Department of Finance Raises Supplementary Budget. In order to supplement the province's construction expenses, the Zhejiang Department of Finance is negotiating with the chambers of commerce and money shops in the five counties of Hangzhou, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Ningbo, and Shaoxing to mortgage construction bonds worth 2.4 million yuan. In addition to directly borrowing 300,000 yuan from the Bank of China, the funds allocated to the various counties for special temporary subsidies and the principal and interest of various loans due are estimated to total about 5 million yuan. It is difficult to raise funds. The department has ordered the sections to investigate and draft a plan for submission to the provincial government meeting for discussion on relief measures.

Settlers to be Transferred in April. The Zhejiang Department of Civil Affairs has notified all counties of the transportation methods and assembly points for immigration and cultivation in the Northeast. It is now known that the department has decided yesterday, for the convenience of assembly and transportation, that the number of people should be reported by the counties at the end of March, and that the immigrants should be transferred from Shanghai to the Northeast at the end of April.

Deadline for Submitting Administrative Plans. The Zhejiang Provincial Government, in accordance with the order of the Executive Yuan, ordered all agencies to pre-order the administrative plans for the whole year and submit them quickly for verification. Yesterday, it specially transferred the order to the various departments, offices, courts, and associations under its jurisdiction. All administrative plans for the whole year of the 19th year and the pre-determined plans for January, February, March and March shall be properly drafted and submitted for verification within ten days of receipt of the document for collection and transfer.

Xiaoshan

Seizure of Guo Huizhen's Private Property. Guo Huizhen, the former magistrate of Xiaoshan County, absconded with funds when the National Army entered Zhejiang. The provincial civil and financial departments ordered an investigation into the deficit, which totaled 61,000 yuan. Guo's ancestral home is Houguan, Fujian. The two departments, believing that the handover was not clear and the deficit was huge, published a notice limiting the payment. They dared to ignore it and were extremely bold. They specially requested the Executive Yuan to transfer the request to the National Government for an explicit arrest and pursuit. They also ordered the local officials in the ancestral home to seize the private property of the magistrate in advance for compensation. Fire in Zhujiatan Village. A fire broke out accidentally in the mansions of the Zhu, Yan, and Chen families in Zhujiatan Village outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan at about 9 p.m. on the 3rd and lasted for two hours. A total of 59 buildings and bungalows were destroyed, and two young children were burned. The loss is more than 40,000 or 50,000 yuan. The disaster victims escaped in single clothes and were injured in falls and burns, which was very tragic.

Shaoxing

Encouraging the Public to Migrate to the Northeast for Cultivation. The Shaoxing County Government received an order from the province yesterday to encourage the public to migrate to the Northeast for cultivation in order to provide relief. County Magistrate Tang ordered the village and neighborhood associations to widely encourage the public. All residents who are willing to immigrate should report their names, ages, and number of people to the county through the associations before March 25 for transfer.

Levying Educational Surcharge on Land Tax. The Shaoxing Education Bureau stated that the educational funds for the 18th year were affected by the land rent, and there was a shortfall of approximately 27,000 yuan compared with the budget. It is now proposed to levy an educational surcharge of one dime and five cents per tael on the land tax, which can increase the annual income by 10,500 yuan. The method has been proposed to the county government meeting for discussion.

Dispatching Personnel to Compile District, Township, and Town Cases. Shaoxing has started to compile district, township, and town cases. The county's territory has been divided into ten districts, and ten commissioners, including Zhang Shouqi, have been appointed as autonomous instructors in each district. All village and neighborhood associations will be abolished after the compilation of district, township, and town cases is completed.
