Local News

Police Rights in 洋棧 of Pudong Are All Recovered

Taigu, Dalai, etc. Have Been Recovered in Order

Britain and the United States Agreed on a Phased Recovery Method

Zhang Mingqin, the third district chief of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, previously reported to Director Yuan that the foreign merchants and factories in the Pudong Yanpu area hired patrolmen or Indian police, which hindered police rights. Moreover, when a labor dispute occurred in a certain factory last year, the doorman Indian police arbitrarily shot and injured a worker. Therefore, he repeatedly requested Director Yuan to seriously negotiate and strive to recover the police rights of all factories and stacks in order to unify the system. In addition to the police rights of the important Taigu, Dalai, Osaka, Anli, Longmao, Asia, and other foreign stacks, which have been recovered in order, it is now learned that the authorities of the British-American Tobacco Company in Lujiazui have also respected our country's orders and agreed on a phased recovery method, successively transferring the original patrolmen and replacing them with petition police to protect the factory. The details are listed as follows:

Details of the Negotiation Process

The British-American Tobacco Company has two factories and one stack, covering a wide area. It employs a total of 64 Chinese patrolmen, which is the largest number of patrolmen employed in the Yanpu area. They are stationed in the stack to guard it, and they have also hired Jie Enjie, the former director of the third police station of Songhu, as the chief manager, who is not under the command of the local police station. After District Chief Zhang of the third district verified the situation, he reported it to the headquarters and personally negotiated with Landuo (transliteration), the general manager of the company, and the British-American Trade Union provided assistance. Due to other waves, it was delayed and not resolved. District Chief Zhang believed that the recovery of police rights was an important matter and could not be allowed to be rejected by foreigners. Therefore, on the 28th of last month, he re-entered the factory to negotiate and repeatedly explained the significance of transferring patrolmen to petition police. After long negotiations, the manager finally agreed to return the police rights to our country and agreed on a phased recovery method to implement it in order. The company refused to allow our country to recover police rights, which has been brewing for a long time, and has only now come to an end.

Phased Recovery Method

District Chief Zhang and the Company

The authorities agreed on a phased recovery method for police rights, which is divided into three phases: the first phase is on the 16th of this month, first transferring all patrolmen in the stack to the district and assigning strong officers and police from the district to protect the stack; the second phase is on April 1st, transferring the patrolmen of the old factory and replacing them with police; the third phase is on April 16th, transferring the patrolmen of the new factory and replacing them with police. After the patrolmen of these three places are replaced by police, the police assigned will be handled in accordance with the temporary regulations for petition police of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. As for the original patrolmen, there were two people in one post. Now, one person will be added to make three police officers in one post. The time was originally six hours on duty and six hours off. It is also changed to three hours on duty and six hours off. The police will be divided into three shifts. If Class A is on duty, Class B will rest, and both shifts will be trained. This will be cycled to balance work and rest.

The Chief Officer Has Been Appointed

The company's original patrolman director, Jie Enjie, was appointed by the Public Security Bureau as the district officer of the Third District Petition Police by Zhang, the district chief, because he had served as the local police chief for many years and was familiar with police affairs. He continued to serve in the factory and was paid according to the salary of the officials of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. An additional patrol officer was added to be responsible for internal and external affairs and all education matters. The Public Security Bureau has now appointed Cui Zhu, the household patrol officer of the district, to fill the position. It is heard that the patrol officer is a graduate of the Beiping Advanced Police Academy and has served in important positions such as the chief of the public security branch. He has considerable experience in police affairs.

Additional Information After the Agreement

The phased recovery of police

After the right method has been agreed, the company has now submitted the clothing fee for the first batch of petition police to the third district, which will be forwarded to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for storage and expedited production of uniforms. The original patrolmen were 64 in number. Now, District Chief Zhang has planned to change all of them to police according to the size of the company and increase the number by 20, for a total of 84, to strengthen the strength. As for the original patrolmen transferred back to the district, the Municipal Public Security Bureau will send personnel to test and separate them. Those who pass will be dressed in police uniforms and reorganized into police, and sent to various places to stand guard to provide training. After the district sends a large number of police to the British-American Company, in addition to using patrolmen to fill the vacancies, the shortage will be supplemented by the training institute of the Municipal Public Security Bureau.

All Sectors Pay Attention to the Case of Stringing Together to Kill One's Step-Mother

Continued Hearing of Zhang Wenqing's Case of Stringing Together to Kill Her Step-Mother

Even More Crowded Attendance at the Hearing Than Before

Bai Wangshi Only Knows the Slang of the Lunar Calendar

The Four Defendants Are Remanded for Another Hearing on the 17th

Almost No Space in the Courtroom

Zhang Wenqing, the eldest daughter of the late Qing official Zhang Fusheng of Huzhou, is 24 years old and unmarried. Due to a dispute over inheritance, she colluded with Chen Hengcai, Yao Yonggui, and Gao Jintang to stab her stepmother Zhang Su to death with a knife at her residence at No. 762 Carter Road at about 6 pm on January 25th of this year. At 2 pm yesterday, Judge Luo Renji, accompanied by American Observer Meng Hate, came to the First Criminal Court of the Temporary Court to continue the hearing. The men and women attending the hearing were even more crowded than before, and there was almost no space in the courtroom.

Both Witnesses Arrived in Court

At around 2 pm, Zhang Wenqing was brought out from the women's prison by an official matchmaker and sat next to the defendant's box, slightly lowering her head. The two lawyers representing the plaintiffs' side, the lawyers Wang Shang and Jiang Baolian representing the defendant Zhang Wenqing, and the lawyer Ru Bao representing the police all arrived on time. First, the police lawyer Ru said that the court had ordered the witnesses Bai Wangshi and Wang Qianshi to be summoned, and the police had now brought the two witnesses to court for questioning.

Wang Qianshi's Testimony

Wang Qianshi then testified, stating that she was from Jiangxi, 27 years old, her husband worked in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and she lived at No. 757 Qing'anli, Avenue Edward VII. She had been neighbors with the Zhang family for seven or eight years. Although they were acquainted on weekdays, they had no contact. At 5:30 pm on January 25th, when Zhang Su was stabbed, she did not know. It was not until around 6 pm that she heard a noise outside. She went out to investigate and saw the deceased sitting on the floor in the living room, bleeding from the head, unable to speak. Her elder wife and eldest daughter (i.e., Wenqing) were standing next to her. Later, the eldest daughter asked me to send her to the hospital. Since there was only the Red Cross Hospital on Carter Road, she and the eldest daughter went to the hospital to contact them, and then came back. The eldest daughter then sent the injured to the hospital in a car. At that time, she did not go with them. At 8 pm, she went to the hospital to visit the injured. At that time, Zhang Wenqing was not there, and the wound had been bandaged by the doctor. She only heard the injured say, "Two children." The injured's sister and her two children were also there. At this point, Judge Luo ordered the four defendants to be taken to the waiting room and ordered the deceased's brother, Su Yaoting, to leave the courtroom for separate questioning. Judge Luo asked Wang Qianshi, "Did the deceased and the elder wife have disagreements on weekdays?" She replied that she did not know. He also asked whether Zhang Wenqing had any unpleasantness with the deceased, and she replied that she did not know. He asked whether Chen Hengcai's mother, who worked for the Zhang family, was fired by the deceased. She replied that she did not know, but after the Zhang family's lawsuit was settled, she was invited to lunch. Some year before, the elder wife told her after she was sick that she had handed over the housework to the mother of the younger Mao Tou (i.e., the deceased) because she was often sick. The deceased also told her that the elder wife had twice wanted to hand over the management rights to her, etc.

The Audience Laughed Loudly

Witness Bai Wangshi testified that she was from Jiangbei, 20 years old, lived in Zhenjiang, and her mother's family lived in Zhabei. The deceased was her maternal aunt and she did not visit often. In November of last year, she went to the Zhang family with the deceased's aunt. Judge Luo asked, "What month did you say, November, lunar or solar?" She replied, "We Jiangbei people only know the lunar calendar and do not know the solar calendar." Those who were listening in the court suddenly laughed loudly. Judge Luo angrily announced, "There are rules for listening in the court. You cannot laugh at will. If you do so again, you will be dealt with according to the law."

Denying the Phrase "Conspiracy to Murder"

He then continued to question Bai Wangshi and testified that it was her first visit in November and that she went again around the 15th of December. Judge Luo asked her, "Zhang Wenqing previously testified that you went to the Zhang family in November and told her that her aunt and her aunt's brother wanted to murder Zhang. Is this true?" She replied, "This is not true." Judge Luo then ordered Zhang Wenqing to be brought to the court for confrontation. Zhang strongly stated that this was true, but Bai Wangshi firmly denied it.

The Issue of Zhang Yin's Accusation

Su Yaoting, the brother of the deceased, was also summoned to the court for questioning. Judge Luo asked, "In your previous statement, in addition to accusing the four defendants in this case, you also accused Zhang Wenqing's brother-in-law, Yin Rongyuan, and sister, Zhang Wenpei, but you have not provided any evidence. In the future, I am afraid that there will be no good results. Do you still accuse them?" Su replied that he would definitely accuse them. The police lawyer Ru immediately stood up and stated that the police had already accused the four defendants. Because there was no evidence against Zhang Wenpei and Yin Rongyuan, they would not be prosecuted. Now that the family of the deceased has filed a lawsuit on their own, a decision should be made first on the progress of this case and whether it should be tried together. Judge Luo reviewed the testimony and said that the family of the deceased had already filed a lawsuit and could not be forcibly stopped. However, the progress of this case and the joint trial are another matter. He hoped that the family of the deceased would withdraw the charges against Zhang Wenpei and Yin Rongyuan, and the plaintiff's lawyer stated that the lawsuit was filed according to the wishes of the parties. As for the evidence, it was unclear. They would discuss it with the parties after the adjournment to determine whether there was sufficient evidence and then make a decision.

Exceedingly Elegant Clothing

Furthermore, Wang Shang, the attorney representing Zhang Wenqing, interrogated Chen Hengcai, asking, "Did you ever hear the deceased plotting to harm Zhang Wenqing?" Chen replied, "At the time, I heard Miss Zhang Wenqing say that if she won the lawsuit, my life would be in danger." He was also asked, "How many days a week was the deceased at home?" He answered, "Only one or two days. The deceased's clothing when going out on weekdays was quite elegant, wearing pink silk cheongsams, etc." The lawyer also asked Zhang Wenqing about the deceased's daily conduct. Zhang replied, "Quite undisciplined, often not returning for several days." At this point in the interrogation, Judge Luo decided that the case still needed to be postponed and instructed the four defendants to be remanded in custody separately, with the retrial scheduled for the afternoon of the 17th of this month.

The Dalun Company Real Estate Lawsuit Was Tried Yesterday

Chinese and foreign real estate industries are paying close attention to this case.

The Chamber of Commerce and the Taxpayers' Association have both sent replies.

The Dalun side presented a great deal of evidence.

The debate was declared closed and a date was set for the verdict.

The Dalun Real Estate Company's lawsuit, due to the refusal of tenants such as the Laoda Fang on Nanjing Road to vacate their premises, has been appealed by Laoda Fang and others, who disagree with the judgment of the Provisional Court in the first instance. They raised three "customs" regarding (1) tenants owing three months' rent, (2) landlords taking back the property for their own use, and (3) old buildings being eligible for reconstruction. The Court of Appeal requested the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee to investigate the existence of these customs to verify the matter. The Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee has now replied to the court. Yesterday afternoon was the date for the retrial of the case. After 2:00 PM, the lawyers and parties of both sides arrived in court successively. The secretary of Mr. Feitang, the consultant to the Public Works Department, and Bo Liang, the lawyer for the police, as well as Chinese and foreign individuals involved in the real estate business, were mostly present in court to observe, given that this case has a significant impact on the future of the real estate industry. Subsequently, Chief Judge Hu, along with Judges Zhong and Zhu, ascended to the bench and had the reply from the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee distributed to the lawyers of both sides for review. The lawyer for the tenants stood up and stated that the reply contained the phrase "in reality, there is no fixed custom," which shows that the custom is not nonexistent. Moreover, the Chinese Taxpayers' Association and the joint chambers of commerce of various roads have also sent letters proving the existence of this custom. The staff of the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee are selected by the Chamber of Commerce Joint Association. Now, the reply from the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee uses ambiguous wording, hastily claiming there is no fixed custom, in hopes of avoiding offending either side. The lawyer also cited a judgment in another rental case, saying that within that judgment, there was also the statement that "even if the property is not taken back for own use, the original tenant still has the right to rent." Renting from Chinese landlords is different from renting from Westerners. When renting from Westerners, there is no need for excavation fees or small rents, while renting from Chinese landlords requires such fees, and so on. Following this, Shi Ying, the lawyer representing Dalun, elaborated in detail on the necessary conditions for the establishment of a custom, listing five points and presenting a great deal of evidence, all of which were procedures used by landlords in the concession for notifying old tenants to vacate when reconstructing new buildings for rent. These were proven by letters from the respective landlords, totaling no fewer than twenty or so, stating that the reasons for those landlords to ask their tenants to move out were mostly similar to the present case, such as the houses not being taken back for own use, nor being old and reconstructed, and there being no so-called right of the old tenants to have priority in renting the new building, etc., and those tenants did not make claims like the tenants in this case. Even the construction of the Sincere, Wing On, and Sun Sun department stores in the past limited tenants to vacating within one month, and the tenants had no objections. Also, Shanghai Bank recently rented land from the Guangzhao Guild Hall to build a house, and its old tenants were all required to vacate within two months. This court was reorganized from the former public office, and the former public office judged a great many rental disputes, but there was no precedent for this custom. Recently, the Yan Maoyuan Hotel was also involved in a property lawsuit, and the result was also a judgment that the tenant vacate, with the judgment containing the statement that "according to a lease contract without a fixed term, the parties can request to terminate the contract at any time." It can be seen that if the tenant does not vacate, there should be a contract, and empty claims cannot be made. Lawyer Qin Liankui, also representing Dalun, argued that what is being disputed now is the issue of custom, and as a result of the investigation by the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee, it was said that there is no fixed custom. No fixed custom naturally means that there is no such custom, and it is definitely not an ambiguous statement. Recently, the appellant's lawyer said that the staff of the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee were appointed by the Chamber of Commerce Joint Association, which is also a misunderstanding. The current Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee is appointed by government order to engage in the reorganization of merchant organizations, equivalent to the General Chamber of Commerce of the past, and its position has nothing to do with the Chamber of Commerce Joint Association or the Taxpayers' Association. The reply from the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee says that there is no such custom, and the only custom claimed by the appellant has no concrete proof, so there is no need for much debate. Another lawyer for the appellant elaborated on the theoretical aspect of the establishment of a custom, then criticized the ambiguity of the reply from the Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee, and then claimed to have investigated and obtained evidence regarding rental disputes from the local court and the municipal government, one being a letter from the county chamber of commerce replying to the local court, and the other being rental rules set by the municipal government, and immediately presented the two items of evidence. The lawyer for Dalun immediately stated that the rules set by the municipal government have not been approved by the central government, so they have not yet taken effect, and attention should be paid to this. After a long debate between the two sides, Chief Judge Hu declared the debate in this case closed and set the date for the verdict at 3:00 PM on the [day missing from original].

Sixty Thousand Dollars in Brand-New Silver Dollars Suddenly Lost in Two Bundles

The dismissed porter displays great skill.

He pried open the silver box and stole two bundles.

He lost two hundred silver dollars gambling in four rounds.

Easy come, easy go.

The Su Hengmao Automobile Freight Company at 214 Boundary Road has been in operation for many years, acting as an agent for various banks, including the Chinese, Communications, and Central Banks in Shanghai, transporting silver for more than ten years. In particular, it has transported newly minted national currency for the Central Bank between Shanghai and Hangzhou in large quantities. Every morning, silver bars are transported from Shanghai to the Hangzhou Mint to be minted into dollars, and in the afternoon, silver dollars are transported back to Shanghai and sent to the Central Bank, which is a common practice. At 12:40 PM yesterday, when the Hangzhou express train arrived in Shanghai, it was also loaded with 60,000 silver dollars, divided into twelve boxes, each containing 5,000 dollars. Each box was sealed on the outside, and the silver dollars inside were further divided into fifty bundles, each containing 100 dollars. After arriving at the station, they were unloaded from the train and temporarily stacked on the platform, then transported out of the station using handcarts, with six boxes per batch. When the porters returned to the platform after loading the first batch of six boxes onto the truck, they suddenly saw that the seal on the top box was broken and the box lid was open, which greatly shocked them. They immediately reported to the company owner, Su Jind, who arrived at the scene. After inspecting the situation, it was discovered that two bundles of silver dollars, totaling 200 dollars, were missing. They immediately inquired whether there were any idlers mixed in while transporting the silver boxes. After some thought, the porters recalled that Xu Yuanshan, a Jiangbei native nicknamed "Little Jiangbei," who had previously worked for the company but had since been dismissed, had been present at the scene. Because they were mostly familiar with him, they did not pay much attention at the time. But when they recalled his lingering near the boxes, it seemed suspicious. Therefore, they reported the information to the Public Concession's Haining Road Police Station and requested them to apprehend him. At the same time, Su Jind hired a car and rushed to Xu Yuanshuang's cake shop at 69 Huaji Road, which was opened by Xu Yuanshan's brother, to investigate. Both Xu's were there. The two brothers were celebrating their windfall, which they could use to gamble for good luck this year. The arrival of the detectives was like a sudden disaster. After the joy, they felt frustrated. According to Xu Yuanshan's confession, he exchanged all of the original 200 dollars for banknotes because he thought it was too heavy to carry. Of those, four dollars had already been lost gambling in a mahjong game on Zhongxing Road. Therefore, the actual amount remaining was 196 silver dollars. Xu Yuanshan and Xu Yuanshuang were both escorted to the police station. The fifth district of the Zhabei Public Security Bureau sent

Page 16

police to bring them back. The defendant confessed to the theft without denying it. Xu Yuanshan confessed that he was 29 years old, from Yangzhou, and had previously worked as a porter at the Su Hengmao Freight Company, but was dismissed for improper behavior and became unemployed. When he pried open the box and committed the theft, it only took five or six minutes. Two hundred brand-new silver dollars were easily obtained, which could be said to be the work of an expert. However, from the time he exchanged the money, lost it gambling, was discovered, and was arrested, it was also only five or six hours, which was also very fast.

A Farmer's Wife Pregnant for Four Months Gives Birth to a Fleshly Egg

The egg contained only a bag of fresh blood.

The family considered it an ominous sign.

Zhang Dada, a resident of the Chongbao Sand area on the border of Baoshan and Chongming counties outside Wusongkou, and his wife, Zhou, who is 34 years old, have been married for over a decade but have not had any children. Zhou is quite virtuous and has repeatedly encouraged her husband to take a concubine to continue the family line, but Zhang has refused because Zhou is not yet old. Unexpectedly, around November of last year, Zhou's menstrual cycle suddenly stopped, which greatly pleased the entire family. Zhou's abdomen grew larger day by day, growing unusually quickly. By the end of last month, only four months had passed, but her abdomen was bulging as if she were ten months pregnant. The family was suspicious and thought that Zhou must be suffering from bloating, so they consulted many doctors for treatment. However, after being diagnosed by general practitioners, they all said that Zhou was indeed pregnant and not ill. Zhang's whole family began to feel at ease, but they were still half-believing and half-doubting. Then, at around 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, Zhou suddenly felt abdominal pain and told her family. Everyone thought that she was only four months pregnant and had not yet reached the time of delivery, so they paid no attention. But at around 2:00 PM, Zhou's abdominal pain became more severe, and in a few minutes, she gave birth to a purple fleshy egg about a foot in diameter, shaped like a soccer ball. The whole family was shocked and the news quickly spread far and wide, with everyone rushing to see it and calling it a strange event. Later, someone claimed that it was probably a wrapped birth, and that if the outer skin of the fleshy egg were cut open, the baby inside could survive. Zhang was afraid of this saying, so he carefully dissected the fleshy egg with a kitchen knife, only to find that the egg contained only a bag of fresh blood and a white, protein-like mucous. In addition to their disappointment, Zhang's family thought it was an ominous sign and immediately threw it into the cesspool. Zhou's spirits were still good after giving birth. This matter is quite unusual and is truly worthy of physiological research.

Children Are Unaware of the Dangers of the Urban Tiger

The Public Security Bureau Reiterates the Prohibition

Instruction: The Municipal Public Security Bureau issued an instruction to all district offices yesterday, stating, "For the purpose of issuing an order, we recently received a letter from Councilor Tang of the Shanghai Special Municipal Government stating that he has witnessed ignorant children playing in the roads every day on his way to Zhabei, rushing back and forth, and even deliberately blocking the way of oncoming cars. If the drivers are not careful, or if the stop is a little late, it can easily cause accidents. If these naughty children are not curbed, it is feared that the number of vehicle-related injuries will inevitably increase day by day. He instructed us to draft measures to curb this phenomenon in order to remedy the situation, etc. In view of this, it has been found that children rushing back and forth on the road can easily cause accidents with passing vehicles if drivers are not careful. A strict prohibition was announced in June of last year, and in December, an order was issued to all district offices to thoroughly investigate and prohibit such behavior. Now, in view of the aforementioned reasons, such incidents still occur in the Zhabei area, and the remaining district offices are likely to be no exception. Although this is due to the people neglecting the prohibition over time, it is also due to the failure of the relevant district offices to implement it effectively. The police have the responsibility of managing traffic and preventing harm, and they should urgently reiterate the previous order and strictly curb such behavior. Subsequently, the heads of the respective district offices should supervise the police officers at all times during their duty or patrols and pay special attention. If they encounter young children deliberately playing and rushing onto the road when cars are approaching, they should still follow the previous order, immediately detain them, summon their parents, order them to discipline their children, and issue a warning. If they re-offend, they will be punished according to the provisions of Article 8, Section 2, Article 42, Section 9 of the Regulations on Punishment of Violations of Police Regulations, and after the immediate decision, the reasons for the punishment will be posted in a concise notice in the area to inform the public and serve as a warning to others. In addition to attaching the announcement prohibiting the behavior and distributing it, the district office director is hereby ordered to promptly comply with and handle this matter, and to post the announcement in appropriate thoroughfares. The locations of the postings should be reported for record. This order."

Announcement: The Municipal Public Security Bureau announces that, considering the heavy traffic and the fast speed of cars, which makes it difficult to stop suddenly, ignorant children often play in the road, and even rush directly at oncoming cars, or even deliberately block the way, which is extremely dangerous. A strict prohibition has already been announced, but people inevitably neglect it over time. Therefore, this is a reiteration of the warning, and the responsibility for discipline lies with the fathers and brothers. If anyone dares to violate the prohibition, they will be punished according to the law.

Shanghai South Public Bus Longhua Line

Adding special buses is pre-announced.

It is customary in this city that during the spring season, merchants and ladies often make appointments to visit Longhua together. The second route of the Shanghai South Public Bus Company's business is at its best during this time of year. The company is now planning to add four to six special buses, converted from the third route circular line buses and designated reserve vehicles that are ready for use, as the existing eight buses are insufficient to meet the demand. These special buses will run from Laoximen, through Xieqiao and Xieshi Road, directly to Longhua, and the fare will be 45 copper coins, which is slightly higher than the regular ticket price, in order to limit ordinary passengers. After the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities submitted the report, it considered that this transfer of buses was aimed at meeting transportation needs and was feasible. However, it instructed that the words "Longhua Special Bus, no stops along the way except for Xieqiao" must be displayed on the outside of the bus and at each stop to avoid disputes caused by short-distance passengers misunderstanding. Also, if the third route circular line is approved for operation, then those buses will still be transferred back to the third route. It is said that the period of operation for these special buses is one month, but the company has not yet set the start and end dates, so the Bureau of Public Utilities has instructed it to submit a supplementary report for record.

Provisional Court Judge Will Inspect the "Fearless" Film

After the screening of the "Fearless" talkie starring Locke at the Da Guangming Cinema, it aroused indignation among the Chinese people, who expressed their opinions and requested the municipal party headquarters to ban it, as has been reported in the newspapers repeatedly. Now, Mr. Hong Shen has formally filed a lawsuit against the Cantonese manager of the cinema, and the Provisional Court, which is handling the case, believes that it is necessary to inspect the "Fearless" film that caused the dispute. It is said that the judge in charge plans to go to the Da Guangming Cinema next Sunday to have the film screened in order to see the whole picture and understand the content. Therefore, Hong Shen's lawsuit must wait until the film has been inspected by the judge before a date for the trial can be set.

Xinzhuang Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Will Install Electric Lights

Xinzhuang Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway is a transportation hub for major towns such as Sijing, so the passenger traffic on each train is extremely crowded. When passengers get on and off the night express train, the platform is dark due to the lack of electric lights, and many people have fallen into the tracks as a result. There have been complaints from the public. The stationmasters of the station, Huang Xun and Fang Yangzhi, aware of this situation, submitted a request to the traffic department to install electric lights, which has been approved, and workers will be dispatched to install them soon.

Continued Report on Ding Runxiang Being Beaten by a Russian

The Medical Examiner's Certificate of Injury

Ding Files a Complaint with the Court

The incident in which Ding Runxiang, the owner of the Paris Cinema on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, was beaten and injured by Keremiruf, a Russian civil servant sent by the Procuratorate of the French Concession Mixed Court, on February 27th of last month (February), has already been reported in this newspaper on the 3rd of this month. Now there is a medical examiner's certificate of injury and the original text of Ding Runxiang's complaint to the French Court, which are recorded below.

Translation of the Certificate of Injury: I, Lang Pei, Medical Officer and Doctor of Medicine from the University of Paris, hereby certify that I examined Mr. Ding Runxiang on February 27, 1930, and found the following injuries: (1) The left eye and lower eyelid are abnormally swollen, with two wounds, one about two centimeters long and the other a straight line, penetrating deep inside the corner of the eye. The two wounds were caused by excessive bleeding and were sewn up by ophthalmologist Yakes. However, according to Yakes' diagnosis, after this eye injury, it is feared that its original function cannot be guaranteed. (2) There is a wound on the lower lip, with a lot of bleeding, and the upper teeth are also injured and swollen. (3) There are many injuries all over the body, especially on the right flank, right elbow, and chest. (4) The injured person vomited blood after being injured, which was very dangerous. Under examination of the lungs, old wounds were clearly seen to have recurred as a result. The above-mentioned injuries were all caused by being assaulted. Signed, Police Officer Ming Pei'an, February 27, 1930.

Original Text of the Complaint: Complainant: Ding Runxiang; Defendant: Keremiruf; Subject: Drunk Assault Causing Injury, Requesting Legal Action and Reserving the Right to Claim Damages. The complainant, Ding Runxiang, was injured in an unprovoked drunk assault by Keremiruf, a bailiff of the French Court, on the 27th of this month. The circumstances of the incident at the time are described as follows: At 11:30 AM that morning, the defendant went to the Paris Cinema to deliver a pre-trial attachment order to the manager, Han Binyi, in a case where Baukes accused the complainant of damage compensation. At that time, Han Binyi was not in the cinema, so the cinema staff led the defendant to a nearby shop to meet Han Binyi. Han received and read the ruling, and said that he had never known about the content of the case, so he wanted to ask Ding Runxiang. He and the defendant Keremiruf returned to the cinema to the room where the complainant lived on the roof garden, told Keremiruf to wait outside, and knocked on the door, preparing to enter the room alone. Unexpectedly, Keremiruf followed him in. At that time, the complainant had not yet gotten out of bed. When he saw Han and others, he got up in his underwear to meet them. Keremiruf explained his purpose, and the complainant asked him to contact his agent, Lawyer Tickbeck. Unexpectedly, Keremiruf raised his fist and punched him. In order to defend himself, the complainant had no choice but to resist. However, Keremiruf was strong and fierce, and dragged the complainant to the cement floor on the roof, where he punched and kicked him. The complainant was covered in injuries, and his right eye was particularly badly injured. Han Binyi was on the scene at the time and wanted to step forward to mediate, but he was also pushed away by Keremiruf. Unable to do anything else, he tried his best to call for help. Fortunately, the cinema staff heard the noise and gathered together, and finally rescued the complainant, while Keremiruf still intended to escape. The three Chinese police officers who arrived at the scene held him down and investigated everything. At first, they planned to arrest Keremiruf, but the Western police officers who arrived at the scene recognized him as a bailiff of the court, so they allowed him to turn himself in to the police station. The complainant's left eye had been injured and was bulging outwards. His family sent him to Pushi Road Hospital, where he was examined by Dr. Lang Pei'an and ophthalmologist Wukesen, but they could not guarantee that the original function of his left eye would be restored. The defendant's intentional injury, regardless of his status, is not permitted by law and should be held criminally responsible without a doubt. Therefore, I hereby file a complaint, requesting that the defendant be ordered to appear in court and be punished for the crime he deserves, and that the plaintiff be allowed to bring a private prosecution, ordering Keremiruf to compensate for all damages caused by the injury, the amount of which will be determined after an assessment. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai French Concession Mixed Court.

The Manager of Guangrentang Pharmacy Turns Himself In and Admits to Arson

Sentenced to Seven Years of Imprisonment

The Guangrentang Pharmacy at No. 2025 Avenue Haig (Avenue d'Eivry) suddenly caught fire at 7:00 PM on December 30th of last year. After the fire brigade extinguished the fire, the police in charge discovered that the pharmacy was involved in insurance fraud. While investigating, Zheng Zhaoxiang, a 60

one-year-old Anhui native, turned himself in to the police, admitting that he was the manager of the pharmacy. Zheng was then sent to the Provisional Court, where he was interrogated repeatedly. He was found to have committed arson. Yesterday morning, Judge Luo opened the court and pronounced the verdict, sentencing Zheng Zhaoxiang to seven years of imprisonment. The number of days spent in detention before the verdict was allowed to be counted as two days for one day.

The Heavenly Incense Ceremony at Longhua

Writing petitions from door to door amounts to thousands of dollars.

A tall wooden frame is built to burn the petitions.

The police bureau bans it as it involves superstition.

Li Bingzhi, 45 years old, from Xiangxiang, Hunan, established the Hua Moral Society and the Haohua Cunchantang in a house at No. 2371 Maogong Bridge, Longhua Road, two years ago. He colluded with the local blind man Cheng Chongguang as a partner and conspired with local ruffians such as Tang to solicit petitions from door to door, amounting to thousands of dollars. Recently, he came up with a bizarre idea. The day before yesterday, he hired workers to build a wooden frame 36 feet tall on an open space in Jijiawan, poured it with kerosene, placed a pot of sandalwood on top, and piled up tree branches and ignition materials below. Then, he burned a paper with the names of the donors on the sandalwood. The fire burned from top to bottom for a Heavenly Incense Ceremony. At the time, smoke filled the sky and flames soared. It was said that it could eliminate disasters and bring blessings, and bring peace to the whole area. Hundreds of ignorant villagers went to worship, and passersby flocked to Longhua Road to watch. The incident was learned by Zheng Pengfei, a patrolman from the Longhua Town Public Security Bureau's branch office, who considered that this kind of action was a form of superstition, and was deeply afraid that it would spread to houses, and that the large number of people would cause chaos and affect public safety. So, he personally led several police officers to disperse the crowd, and made every effort to extinguish the fire and demolish the wooden frame. Li Bingzhi, Dan Shichang, and two other people, who were the ringleaders, were taken back to the station. After a brief interrogation, he thought that these people were spreading rumors to confuse the public and using it as a pretext to collect money, so he immediately prepared a document and sent them to the Sixth District, Third Precinct for handling.

Huashang and Zhabei Two Electrical Companies

Change the Electricity Supply Areas of Fahua and Pusong

The three districts of Fahua, Caoging, and Pusong in this city were not originally within the operating area of any electrical company. In order to implement the policy of universal electricity supply, the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities had submitted requests to the Municipal Government in May and June of the 18th year and obtained approval to temporarily assign the entire territory of the three districts to the Huashang and Zhabei two electrical companies for electricity supply, respectively. After the plan was finalized, the area around Xujiahui Catholic Church, which had been supplied with electricity by the French Concession, was officially taken back and supplied by the Huashang Electrical Company. The electricity use in Fahua Town is also being planned for distribution by the company. As for the Pusong district, the Beixinjing Town was also electrified by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company at the end of January of this year. In the future, the electricity supply in the three districts will meet the needs and will expand more and more widely. It can be said with certainty that, in terms of location, Caoging District is located in the southeast, close to the operating area of the Huashang Electrical Company, so it is appropriate to assign it to Huashang. However, Fahua and Pusong districts, one in the east and one in the west, at that time, the bureau aimed to make the operating area consistent with the administrative area for easy supervision, so it assigned Fahua to Huashang and Pusong to Zhabei. This division method can be called the east-west division method. However, according to the inherent operating areas of the Huashang and Zhabei companies, one is in the south and one is in the north, and the Fahua and Pusong districts are located in between. The southern part is close to Huashang, and the northern part along the south bank of the Suzhou River is close to Zhabei. If we do not adhere to the administrative area, but consider the convenience of connecting wires and supplying electricity, then it is appropriate to assign the northern part of the two districts to Zhabei and the southern part to Huashang. Moreover, within the two districts, the roads built by the Public Concession across the border are crisscrossed. If Huashang wants to pass through these roads to supply electricity to the northern part of Fahua District, and Zhabei wants to pass through these roads to supply electricity to the southern part of Pusong District, in fact, there will be many disputes, and the equipment will not be economical. In view of this, the bureau also found that there is Daxilu in Fahua District and Hongqiao Road in Pusong District, both of which run from east to west, right in the middle of the north and south. Therefore, it suggested to the Municipal Government to change to the north-south division method, using Daxilu and Hongqiao Road as the boundary, dividing the Fahua and Pusong districts into northern and southern parts. The southern part is assigned to Huashang, and the northern part is assigned to Zhabei. In this way, the operating scope of both parties will not be greatly affected, and the connection and electricity supply will be much more convenient. It will also have no impact on the current electricity supply situation of the two companies in the two districts. It is said that the Municipal Government considers this method of changing the electricity supply area feasible and has instructed that it be approved.

The Problem of Foreign Silver Import Tax Is Undecided

Due to the impact of soaring gold prices and plummeting silver prices, the National Government authorities have had various plans, among which the two most prevalent are the prohibition of foreign silver imports and the imposition of heavy taxes on foreign silver imports. In recent days, various markets have been rumored that the National Government will implement a plan to impose heavy taxes on foreign silver imports, and that it will be implemented starting next week. According to investigations from various sources, the National Government has not yet decided on a solution to the above plan. It is currently being jointly reviewed by Minister Kong of Industry and Commerce and Minister Song of Finance. How it will be expressed, there is no decision yet. External rumors are all speculations by speculators, and the National Government will have a formal order announced.

Customs Brokerage Industry Requests Reduced Water Freight Charges Again

The Shanghai North and South City Customs Brokerage Association sent letters yesterday to China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Taikoo Dockyard, Ning Shao Steamship Company, and Sanpei Shipping Company, stating: "We are writing to you because we received a letter from the Ningbo Anlan Association, and we were also informed by dozens of North and South Goods and Sugar businesses that the cost of some of these goods is relatively low, and they cannot afford to increase the water freight charges. Otherwise, they will be forced to use other transportation routes. Therefore, they entrusted our association to negotiate with your four companies to modify the water freight charges so that both parties can benefit."

"We commissioned Committee Member Zhou Jingzhai to investigate whether this was true. Now, according to Committee Member Zhou's reply, there are fifty or sixty types of sugar, North and South goods, all of which are food products and cannot be compared to luxury goods. For those with higher costs, the stipulated water freight charges are still manageable. However, there are eight types of goods with very low costs: rock sugar, melon seeds, jujubes, bean starch noodles, peanuts, walnuts, raw kernels, and sesame seeds. Each load only costs between ten and eight taels of silver, and it is difficult to sustain with the increased water freight charges. It will inevitably lead to the cessation of transportation by steamships and a switch to sailboats. This will result in losses for both the transportation company and the North and South goods businesses."

"This matter concerns the interests of all three parties. We urge your company to consider improvements so that business can be sustained for a long time. We hope you will carefully consider this matter. We are writing to inform you accordingly, and we hope you will investigate and take appropriate action."

Meeting Report of the Chinese Child Welfare Association

The Children's Research Department Actively Implements the Original Plan: The Shanghai Chinese Child Welfare Association has drafted a child protection law. However, it is necessary to further study how to protect children. Therefore, the Children's Research Department Committee of the association convened a meeting at the association's headquarters the other day. Attendees included Mr. Chuan Ruoyu (Chairman), Dr. Fu Wenshou, and Professor Chen Heqin. The following was decided to implement the department's original plan: (1) Establish a child welfare library; (2) Investigate the physical, intellectual, and dynamic development of Chinese children, and seek a norm for development as a guideline for future child welfare undertakings; (3) Investigate the latest methods of child rearing and parent training in various countries, as well as various designs for the benefit of children, and compile them systematically with the essence of China's inherent culture to introduce them to Chinese parents and those enthusiastic about child welfare; (4) Print and distribute single-page forms, booklets, and monthly publications to promote and accelerate progress. In addition, to gather wisdom and recruit talent to implement the plan, the department has specially invited Section Chief Zhu Zhanggeng of the Municipal Health Bureau and Mr. Wei Sibo, former Dean of Academic Affairs of Shanghai University, to serve as committee members.

Divorce Case Settled in Court

Mrs. Xu Gu, 26 years old, a native of Shanghai, residing in Lujiawan, married Xu Sifu, a carpenter from Nan Shoumu Bridge in Yinxianggang, at the age of 20. After the marriage, the couple was not harmonious and she was not favored by her mother-in-law. Therefore, she had to live temporarily at her mother's house, while Xu went to other places to do business. This situation has lasted for seven years. At the end of last year in the lunar calendar, the case was once involved in a police station dispute. Now, Mrs. Xu Gu has hired a lawyer to file a divorce lawsuit with the District Court, stating briefly: "The plaintiff used to work in a yarn factory and married the defendant on March 24th of the Republic of China's 13th year. At that time, I only knew that the defendant was a carpenter who could support himself. But after the marriage, the defendant did not engage in production, and his mother was especially violent. Every time the factory paid wages, she would ask the plaintiff for her wages. If she was not satisfied, the mother and son would unite and either beat or scold her. The plaintiff could not bear the suffering and had to live temporarily at her mother's house, while the defendant would come to harass her from time to time. He even injured the plaintiff's mother. Later, the plaintiff was persuaded to return to the defendant's house, but the defendant and his mother continued to mistreat her, even detaining the plaintiff's clothes. The plaintiff had to return to her mother's house. These events all happened in the 13th year. In June of last year, the plaintiff's mother passed away. In August, the plaintiff's second sister, Zhou Gu, came and claimed that the defendant was demanding a divorce from the plaintiff, asking for 200 yuan in compensation. The plaintiff refused his request. On December 28th, the second sister came with detectives and claimed that the defendant had accused the plaintiff of embezzlement at the 2nd District Branch. She was ordered to be arrested and taken to the branch, then transferred to the 2nd District for detention. Her eldest sister, Sun Gu, bailed her out. On February 13th of the solar calendar, detectives suddenly came again and arrested the eldest sister, Sun Gu, for detention, but she was later released. The plaintiff only seeks to escape the entanglement and does not want to create further complications. Therefore, she requests unconditional divorce."

The defendant also hired lawyer Hu Yuanjun to file a defense and counterclaim, requesting cohabitation, briefly stating: "After marrying the plaintiff, the relationship was initially harmonious. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff was unfaithful and incited by her sister, Sun Gu. On December 23rd of the 13th year, she fled without a trace and could not be found after repeated searches. It was not until last year that her address was discovered, and the police were informed to arrest her. Soon after, her sister bailed her out, stating that Gu would return home. On January 9th, she went to the station to inquire, and the district informed her of the bail situation, so Sun Gu was again detained. Now, Xu Gu, deceived by Sun Gu, has filed a lawsuit requesting divorce. The defendant strongly opposes it and requests cohabitation."

Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang opened the court for trial. Both parties arrived in court with their lawyers and successively stated the previous events. The plaintiff insisted on divorce, while the defendant requested cohabitation. The judge repeatedly advised the plaintiff and instructed the defendant not to mistreat her. The plaintiff said, "They want to chain me up." The judge said, "If they chain you, you are allowed to come and report it." Thus, a settlement was reached. The plaintiff voluntarily agreed to wait two more days, and the defendant would go to pick her up and reunite. Both parties signed the agreement and adjourned the court.

Difficult to Guard Against a Wife

Enticed Away by a Fellow Villager in Hankou

Intercepted by Detectives in Shanghai

Ms. Xu Xinbao, 21 years old, from Zhoupu, Pudong, was betrothed to Yao Yuping, a fellow villager. Yao, 24 years old this year, works in Wu Guisheng's leather suitcase shop on Houchang Road in Hankou. After Yao returned to his hometown to marry her the year before last, the newlyweds only enjoyed ten days before he was forced to leave his hometown due to livelihood concerns. Fearing that his young and beautiful wife would be alone and vulnerable to improper incidents, he disregarded the high cost of living in the city and brought his beloved wife to Hankou to live together so that they could see each other day and night and be easily supervised. However, things did not go as planned. In December of last year, Qian Ruixiang, 25 years old, also from Pudong, worked as a carpenter for foreigners in Hankou. He knew both Yao and Xinbao. Meeting a fellow villager in a foreign land, their relationship was unusually warm, and they often visited each other, which led to bringing a wolf into the house. Qian and Xinbao fell in love, and the matter gradually leaked out. Xinbao was blamed by her husband, and they could no longer coexist. Qian and Xinbao packed up their belongings and fled to Shanghai on the Ruiyang steamboat. Because they were not formally married, their actions appeared awkward, which was noticed by the accountant, who investigated and questioned them, leading to exposure. Therefore, yesterday, when the ship arrived at the port, a phone call was made to the Relief Society, and investigators Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang boarded the ship to inquire, leading to a full confession. They were arrested and taken to the Water Police Station. Detective Cheng Yongnian was immediately dispatched to take Qian and Xinbao to the District Court. After an interrogation by the prosecutor, Qian was ordered to be detained, and Xu Xinbao was sent to the Relief Society for custody, awaiting her husband's arrival for further verification. However, when the prosecutor questioned Xu Xinbao about her age, because those under 20 years old are considered victims of abduction, he asked her when her birthday was. Surprisingly, Xinbao did not even know her own birthday, which is also a strange occurrence.

Gamblers Arrested from Inside a Coffin

Every night, people gathered to gamble at the Shun Da Wood Company on Wusong Outer Ma Road. This was discovered by the 7th District Public Security Bureau. The other night, at around 11 o'clock, Inspector Dai Guosheng led more than ten policemen to secretly make arrests. Upon arriving at the destination, they found that the fence gate around the company was already tightly closed, making it impossible to enter. They climbed over the fence and entered. When the gamblers saw the arrest, they all fled from the back. The inspector ordered the policemen to guard the gate and search everywhere. Soon, in the coffin storeroom, which also served as a workshop, they shone a flashlight and suddenly saw a coffin lid moving automatically. The policemen were surprised and suspicious, so they stepped forward and opened the coffin lid. To their surprise, the gamblers jumped out of the coffin one after another. They were immediately arrested one by one and taken back to the station for interrogation.

Drunk Man Falls into the River While Crossing and Drowns

Jiang Ziyuan, from Xinzhuang, worked as a partner at the Zhenli Fujian Firm in Nanshi. Yesterday, he borrowed 15 yuan from the firm and went out, telling his colleagues that he was going to a relative's house in Zhoujiadu to participate in a hui (rotating credit association). Unexpectedly, Jiang suddenly met a friend at the South Wharf, and they went to a restaurant to drink together. Heavily drunk, his friend could not dissuade him. Jiang, fearing that he would miss the hui date, hired a boat to cross the river to Pudong. Upon arriving at the Pudong Wharf, he somehow fell into the water. The boatman could not rescue him. Later, a coal boat found his body at the Ri Hui Port. The firm learned of this and went to identify the body, confirming that it was him. They prepared a coffin and took it away, and also informed Jiang's family in Xinzhuang. The coffin was transported back. It is said that Jiang was 24 years old and had an old mother, a wife, two sons, and one daughter.

Apprentice Hangs Himself on the Upper Floor

Ruan Fugen, 14 years old this year, the second grandson of Ruan Heshan (74 years old) from Gaojiagang, Pudong, was an apprentice in the pawnshop opened by his relative Gu Hongqing (No. 106 Zhengjia Muqiao Street). The child was cheerful and kind and never had any disputes with anyone in the shop. It is unknown why Fugen suddenly had a pessimistic idea. The other day, at 2 p.m., he went upstairs, took an old horse bellyband, and hanged himself at the stairwell. It was not until the senior apprentice Qu Decheng went upstairs to check packages that he caught a glimpse of him. Greatly alarmed, he ran downstairs and told the shop owner, who went upstairs to check. Ruan's face was pale, and it was too late to save him. He had already died. The shop owner reported it to the French Police Station, which ordered detectives to go. They transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall morgue for examination. Meanwhile, Gu sent someone to the countryside to urge the deceased's grandfather to come to Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon, Zhu, the judge of the Criminal Division of the French Court, arrived at the scene and confirmed that the deceased had indeed died by hanging himself. He ordered the family of the deceased to prepare a coffin and take it away with the shop owner.

The Septic Tank in the Xue Family Garden Has Not Yet Been Renovated

Sentenced to a Fine of 25 Yuan

The French Municipal Council previously accused Xue Baorun, a wealthy businessman from Xiafei Road, in the French Court of not demolishing the septic tank in his garden, which was detrimental to sanitation. He was ordered to renovate the septic tank into a Western-style toilet. Yesterday, he was summoned again. An official from the Municipal Council stated first that the defendant had ignored the order and obviously intended to defy the court's order. He requested an investigation. The defendant was notified, and someone named A substituted him and gave evasive testimony. The Chinese and Western judges ruled that the defendant should not have defied the court's order and fined him 25 yuan to be confiscated. The Public Works Bureau will still supervise the renovation.

Actually, Nothing Happened

Please make a decision on the case. It was resolved and passed. The meeting adjourned.

Small Fire at Jiang Yanze Pharmacy

At around 3 p.m. yesterday, a fire broke out in the Jiang Yanze Medicinal Materials Store at No. 444 Main Street, outside the Xiaonanmen, Shanghai. Damp medicinal materials were being dried on a stove in preparation for making medicine. Unexpectedly, due to carelessness, the fire spread to the nearby medicinal materials, and thick smoke and flames quickly filled the air. In a moment, the fire broke through the roof. The Firefighting Association was nearby and immediately sounded the alarm upon seeing it. Fire brigades from various districts quickly drove pumping trucks to the scene and poured water to extinguish the fire. It took some time to put out the fire. Only one bungalow of the store was destroyed, and the rest was not affected. Afterward, Liu Jinghe, the guard of the 10th post of the association, arrived and took Lu Peiyuan, a Ningbo native and a store employee, to the 1st District 3rd Branch, where Director Jin ordered him to be detained for review.

Two Announcements from the Maritime Affairs Section and the Inspection and Construction Division

The Maritime Affairs Section and the Inspection and Construction Division of the Customs issued an announcement: This Inspection and Construction Division has investigated the location of the Jinpai Gate Zhongsha Lower Buoy under the jurisdiction of the Customs Commissioner of the Minhai Customs and its shifting position. The situation is listed on the left. The Jinmen Zhongsha Lower Buoy in the Minjiang River will be moved around March 8. It will be implemented at that time, and no further notice will be given. It will be moved about 400 feet south from its original location (according to the compass direction). The rest of the situation remains the same. The water depth at the parking place is 20 feet when the neap tide recedes. All nautical charts No. 6 issued by the Maritime Affairs Bureau should be corrected immediately. Therefore, all ships should be notified to comply with this announcement, pay attention to details, and avoid negligence. Do not forget, do not neglect, be sure of this announcement. February 4, Republic of China Year 19.

Another announcement said: This Inspection and Construction Division has investigated and reported shallow water within the jurisdiction of the Customs Commissioner of the Chaozhou Customs. The situation is listed on the left. According to the report, the shallow sand in the inner harbor of Shantou has expanded. When the neap tide recedes, the water depth in the waterway is only 17 feet. Refer to British Navy Admiralty Chart No. 854 for clarity. Education News

Important News

Implementation of the Party's Education Policy Proposal (Continued)

Methods

1. General Principles: (1) The Ministry of Education shall organize an Obligatory Education Committee and a Vocational Education Committee to be responsible for planning and implementing national obligatory education, adult supplementary education, and vocational programs, and to determine implementation procedures, to be carried out in stages and effectively. (2) Educational administrative organs in all provinces and counties shall employ experts to organize Obligatory Education Committees and Vocational Education Committees to assist and supervise the planning and implementation of various projects. (3) All facilities for national obligatory education and adult supplementary education should develop the following essential elements: 1. Life skills; 2. Civic qualifications; 3. National consciousness; 4. Healthy body and mind. (4) Vocational education should focus on cultivating practical and technical talent; specialized talent should also be emphasized. (5) Determine the independent status of normal schools in the school system and make independent establishment the principle.

2. National Obligatory Education: (1) The term of national obligatory education shall be fixed at six years. (2) Tuition fees should be waived during the period of obligatory education, and textbooks and learning supplies should be provided by the public. (3) Enact a compulsory obligatory education law, laws on rewards and punishments for parents of school-age children, laws on rewards and punishments for county magistrates and educational administrators, and laws on encouraging donations for education, etc., to ensure effective compulsory enforcement. (4) The number of out-of-school children in all regions should be reduced by at least 20 percent every two years, with the aim of completely universal education within ten years. (5) Obligatory education expenses shall be borne jointly by the central government, provincial regions, and county cities. Special increases in subsidies should be provided for counties and districts in impoverished areas.

3. Adult Supplementary Education: 1. Adult supplementary education should be differentiated according to occupation, level, and age (such as farmers' supplementary schools and workers' supplementary schools, those who have received education and those who have not, each having different requirements), with the provinces determining the length of education to be received. 2. In addition to being required to be attached to elementary schools, adult supplementary schools should make use of temples, ancestral halls, guild halls, and other public places to establish schools widely. 3. Enact laws and regulations stipulating that factories or shops employing 40 or more people should establish supplementary schools, with the expenses borne by the factory owners, shop owners, or shareholders. 4. Educational administrative organs in all counties and cities should widely establish public reading rooms, public sports fields, popular libraries, mobile libraries, etc., and should also make use of broadcasting, movies, drama, and lantern slides to supplement adult education. 5. The planning of expenses for adult supplementary education shall be the same as that for national obligatory education, and the treatment of students shall also be the same. 6. Each province should divide regions to establish adult supplementary education teacher training institutes, recruiting normal school and middle school graduates and elementary school teachers who volunteer for service, providing them with short-term training to create teachers for adult education. 7. The treatment of adult education teachers should be the same as that of elementary school teachers, and those who also serve as elementary school teachers should receive additional subsidies. 8. Enact compulsory supplementary education laws and stipulate that relevant staff and service personnel of all agencies should give priority to hiring those who have received supplementary education as a means of encouragement.

4. Normal School Education: (1) Normal schools should be changed to a four-year system, recruiting junior high school graduates. (2) In order to meet the special needs of rural villages, each province should consider establishing rural normal schools, recruiting junior high school graduates and those with equivalent education levels, with a study period of two years or more. (3) Normal schools should have the facilities of experimental elementary schools, and rural normal schools should designate appropriate farms and villages for experimental use. (4) Normal school students should receive strict military training and have the necessary technical knowledge of local production industries. (5) Normal schools should add subjects related to adult education for the purpose of serving concurrently as adult normal schools. (6) Tuition and other fees for normal schools should be completely waived. (7) Laws and regulations should be formulated to protect the graduates of normal schools and to increase the salaries of elementary school teachers. (8) Training classes should be established during vacations to provide training for incumbent elementary school teachers and private tutors year by year. Teachers or tutors who are unqualified and unwilling to receive training should be strictly suppressed.

5. Vocational Education: (1) Vocational schools of all levels should be established in industrial areas, with the aim of improving local craftsmanship and increasing industrial production. (2) Industrial schools must have experimental factories attached and must focus on practical training, with academic subjects as supplementary. (3) The country should be divided into several agricultural zones, with one agricultural college established in each zone, and agricultural schools established in various places. Within the school zone, agricultural experimental farms and local rural normal schools, rural elementary schools, agricultural cooperatives, etc., should be connected to each other, and agricultural extension workers should be stationed to guide various villages in the zone, with the aim of increasing agricultural production technology and efficiency. (4) The Ministry of Education and the Training Directorate should jointly plan and implement vocational education for the military. (5) It is stipulated that technical personnel of government agencies should give priority to hiring graduates of vocational schools, and vocational placement agencies should be established in all provinces, counties, and cities to specifically handle introductions and placements.

6. Free Education and Scholarships: (1) Public schools above the secondary level should set up a certain number of free student slots, increasing them year by year, and when the school's funding is sufficient, all students should be free. (2) Private schools above the secondary level should set up a certain number of free student slots, the number of which must not be less than one-tenth of the school's total student slots. Any violation of this provision will result in non-registration. Private schools with outstanding achievements should be subsidized by the state. (3) The central government and provincial, county, and city governments should establish a certain number of scholarships to provide funding for outstanding students to pursue further studies at home and abroad. (4) Those who have scientific writings, research, and inventions should be rewarded handsomely by the state. (5) Those who donate funds for scholarships should be given special awards by the state. (End)

Order Abolishing University Preparatory Courses

The Ministry of Education issued an order to all universities that they should no longer recruit preparatory students from the 19th academic year onwards. If necessary, they may run affiliated senior high schools separately. The order was published in this newspaper on the 6th of this month. The text of the order is recorded below. The establishment of preparatory courses in universities was originally an expedient measure, but universities that have not managed well often have the name of a university, but in reality, preparatory students account for the majority, and the drawbacks are too numerous to mention. According to the University Organization Law, universities are also not allowed to set up preparatory courses. All national, provincial, and private universities shall no longer recruit preparatory students from the 19th academic year onwards. The existing preparatory courses in each school should continue until the students currently enrolled in the preparatory courses have completed their studies. If there are indeed practical difficulties, the universities may be temporarily allowed to run affiliated senior high schools according to local conditions. If there are students who have graduated from the old system of middle schools and intend to take the entrance examination, they should be admitted to the school through the affiliated senior high school and assigned to the appropriate grade according to their level, in order to provide relief. In addition to distributing this order, the universities are hereby ordered to comply. This order.

(2) The farmer entertainment method will be based on the revised draft proposed by Gu Shaoyi of the Ministry of Education. Shanghai University Defeats Jinling in Four Universities Basketball Tournament

Result: 52 to 18

Jinling vs. Soochow Today at 3:00 PM

As the whistle blew, a roar of applause erupted, and the curtain rose on the Four Universities Basketball Championship. Athletic Jinling athletes and skilled Shanghai University players met in the Shanghai University gym. After a fierce battle of 40 minutes and hundreds of rounds of play, Shanghai University defeated Jinling with a score of 52 to 18. Referee: Xu Zhendong. This took place yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the first day of the championship. Today at 3:00 PM, Jinling will play against Soochow. Referee: Zhang Guoxun. The battleground remains the same.

Watching the Basketball Game Causes a Sensation Throughout the School

As the battle between Jinling and Shanghai University was about to begin, the atmosphere throughout Shanghai University suddenly became tense. Male and female students told each other that Jinling had outstanding talent, and this time they were confident of winning and would defeat all the heroes and take the championship trophy. They were afraid that Shanghai University would not be able to retain the honor of last year's championship. Others said that Shanghai University's basketball skills were well-known for their powerful attacks, and although Jinling was strong, they were no match for us. Even if they were not, we, along with our classmates, would come to watch the game in person, cheer together, inspire morale, and boost military morale. At that time, our army's momentum would double its power, and it would not be difficult to destroy the enemy and win. People's opinions differed, but their aspirations were the same, all were related to honor and disgrace, and the great cause was at stake. Therefore, there was a scramble for tickets to the battlefield, and people sat crowded together. The male students sat high up, with a panoramic view, and the female students sat around, with the entire field of vision, the situation of the two teams' battles was fully revealed before the eyes of these enthusiastic and caring students. Only at the beginning did they see their teeth smiling and their expressions calm, because the Shanghai University athletes lived up to expectations and had already exhausted their talents and skills, gaining a superior position. At the same time, the number of people who traveled from afar to watch was also large, and the long-desolate gym suddenly became a hot spot.

Talent Varies in Each Person

Shanghai University has been famous for its basketball for a while. Since He Tong was injured, the center was lacking, and the morale of the army was inevitably worried. It was also rumored from afar that Jinling's strength was strong this year and could not be surpassed, so at the beginning of the war, He Tong still entered the field and fought bravely. By the time the first half ended, Shanghai University had already secured the victory, so they changed their tactics and withdrew themselves. He's performance was difficult to match the magic of the past, but the prestige of Zhang Benjun and the capture of the enemy's spirit were greatly related to his personal performance. Liang Guoquan was smart and lively, leading the entire field. As for his many points and excellent assists, no one can match him. Ouyang Yongyuan has gradually emerged recently. Ouyang is worthy of the saying "One should look at a scholar with new eyes after he has been away three days." Wang Peng's inside guard is wonderful in its combination of rigidity and flexibility, and its balance of offense and defense. Sun Zemin's throwing has created its own style, which is indeed unique. The others can still do their jobs, and the excellent cooperation of the whole team is even more admirable. In short, Shanghai University's victory has three reasons: one is that everyone does their job, two is that the cooperation is excellent, and three is that the field is familiar. When strong enemies meet, having one or two of these is enough to defeat the enemy and win, let alone having all three. The Jinling players are tall and strong, full of spirit. When they stand in the field with heroic posture, they have the ambition that they cannot be surpassed, but unfortunately, the individual's strength is more than enough, and the cooperation of the whole team is not good enough, so they are at a disadvantage and withdraw in defeat. Forward Ling Huiyang appears all over the field, able to attack and defend, and is the pillar of the entire team. Center Tu Zhong takes care of both the front and back, and his throwing and passing are appropriate, and he is also a dangerous person. The rest of the people have both strengths and weaknesses, and their biggest problem is their slow movement. However, the qualifications are all good. Given time and training, they will soon be able to sweep across the battlefield.

Talking About the Great Difference in the Strength of the Battle

The order to declare war was issued, and both sides began to act. Jinling rushed forward fiercely, with great momentum. The morale of the Shanghai University army was terrified and somewhat cramped. The first to break the record of the two teams was Jinling Huiyang, followed by Shanghai University Wang Jinping. Then He Tong and Ouyang each scored one point on a penalty, and soon the situation became seven to five. At that time, Shanghai University occupied the lead, but the entire army's advance and retreat was not wonderful, so they immediately rested, the men devised a good plan, and the sound rang again, and it was effective. From then on, the entire army's arms were connected, and they swept across the field. Jinling tried hard to accelerate, but to no avail. In the first half, Shanghai University took the lead 26 to 10. In the second half, Shanghai University's generals were replaced frequently, and the ball was still strong. Jinling succumbed to the power, and it was difficult to turn around. At one point, Tu Zhongqi even scored three goals, and the situation improved, but the strength of the crossbow at the end was limited, so it soon fell again and could not get up. The result of the match was 52 to 18, a great victory for Shanghai University. Referee: Xu Zhendong.
